{JB, 1, 1}
tat āhuḥ kena juhoti kasmin hūyate iti | [JB, 1, 1 644484_1]
prāṇena eva juhoti | [JB, 1, 1 644485_1]
prāṇe hūyate | [JB, 1, 1 644485_2]
tat yat etat agnīn manthanti prāṇān janayanti | [JB, 1, 1 644486_1]
tat yāvat vai manthanti na tarhi prāṇiti | [JB, 1, 1 644487_1]
araṇyoḥ eva asya tarhi prāṇāḥ bhavanti | [JB, 1, 1 644488_1]
tasya vai mathyamānasya bhasma avaśīyate | [JB, 1, 1 644489_1]
annam eva asya tat jāyate | [JB, 1, 1 644490_1]
annam me etat ajani iti eva tat vidyāt | [JB, 1, 1 644491_1]
dhūmaḥ anu ninardati | [JB, 1, 1 644492_1]
manaḥ eva asya tat jāyate | [JB, 1, 1 644493_1]
manaḥ me etat ajani iti eva tat vidyāt | [JB, 1, 1 644494_1]
aṅgāraḥ anu nirvartate | [JB, 1, 1 644495_1]
cakṣuḥ eva asya tat jāyate | [JB, 1, 1 644496_1]
cakṣuḥ me etat ajani iti eva tat vidyāt | [JB, 1, 1 644497_1]
saḥ eṣaḥ aṅgāraḥ etāni bhasmāni grasate | [JB, 1, 1 644498_1]
yathā kumāraḥ jātaḥ stanam abhipadyeta tathā tiryaṅ visarpati | [JB, 1, 1 644499_1]
śrotram eva asya tat jāyate | [JB, 1, 1 644500_1]
śrotram me etat ajani iti eva tat vidyāt | [JB, 1, 1 644501_1]
upari tṛṇāni dhunoti | [JB, 1, 1 644502_1]
prāṇaḥ eva asya sa jāyate | [JB, 1, 1 644503_1]
prāṇaḥ me eṣaḥ ajani iti eva tat vidyāt | [JB, 1, 1 644504_1]
bhās iti uddīpyate | [JB, 1, 1 644505_1]
vāc eva asya sā jāyate | [JB, 1, 1 644506_1]
vāc me eṣā jani iti eva tat vidyāt | [JB, 1, 1 644507_1]
saḥ etān pañca prāṇān janayate | [JB, 1, 1 644508_1]
tān tredhā vyūhya devān kṛtvā teṣu juhvat āste | [JB, 1, 1 644509_1]
devāḥ ha eva asya devāḥ bhavanti | [JB, 1, 1 644510_1]
ime tu eva asya devāḥ bhavanti yeṣu juhvat āste | [JB, 1, 1 644511_1]
{JB, 1, 2}
tat yat āhuḥ kena juhoti kasmin hūyate iti prāṇena eva juhoti prāṇe hūyate | [JB, 1, 2 644512_1]
tat etat annam prāṇe juhoti | [JB, 1, 2 644512_2]
imān hi prāṇān abhivardhayamānaḥ teṣu juhvat āste | [JB, 1, 2 644513_1]
atha etat ha vāva brāhmaṇasya svam yat haviḥ | [JB, 1, 2 644514_1]
tat ātman nidhatte eṣu amṛteṣu prāṇeṣu | [JB, 1, 2 644515_1]
tat asya ātman nihitam na pramīyate | [JB, 1, 2 644516_1]
yadā vai manaḥ utkrāmati yadā prāṇaḥ yadā cakṣuḥ yadā śrotram yadā vāc etān eva agnīn abhigacchati | [JB, 1, 2 644517_1]
atha asya idam śarīram eteṣu eva agniṣu anupravidhyanti | [JB, 1, 2 644518_1]
asmāt vai tvam ajāyathāḥ eṣa tvat jāyatām svāhā iti | [JB, 1, 2 644518_2]
saḥ atas āhuti mayaḥ manaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa mayaḥ cakṣuḥ mayaḥ śrotra mayaḥ vāc mayaḥ ṛk mayaḥ yajuḥ mayaḥ sāma mayaḥ brahma mayaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ amṛtaḥ sambhavati | [JB, 1, 2 644519_1]
amṛtāḥ ha eva asya prāṇāḥ bhavanti | [JB, 1, 2 644520_1]
amṛta śarīram idam kurute | [JB, 1, 2 644521_1]
saḥ amṛta tvam gacchati yaḥ evam vidvān agnihotram juhoti | [JB, 1, 2 644522_1]
{JB, 1, 3}
prajāpatiḥ sahasra saṃvatsaram āsta | [JB, 1, 3 644523_1]
sa sapta śatāni varṣāṇām samāpya imām eva jitim ajayat yā asya iyam jitiḥ tām | [JB, 1, 3 644524_1]
sa svargam lokam ārohan devān abravīt etāni yūyam trīṇi śatāni varṣāṇām samāpayātha iti | [JB, 1, 3 644525_1]
tathā iti | [JB, 1, 3 644526_1]
te trīṇi śatāni varṣāṇām samāpya tām u eva jitim ajayan yām prajāpatiḥ ajayat | [JB, 1, 3 644527_1]
te ete sarve eva prajāpati mātrāḥ ayam ayam iti | [JB, 1, 3 644528_1]
te abruvan deva śarīraiḥ vai idam amṛta śarīraiḥ samāpāma na vai idam manuṣyāḥ samāpsyanti eta imam yajñam saṃbharāma iti | [JB, 1, 3 644529_1]
tam saṃvatsaram abhisamabharan | [JB, 1, 3 644532_1]
te abruvan mahat vai idam sam eva bharāma iti | [JB, 1, 3 644533_1]
tam dvādaśa aham abhisamabharan | [JB, 1, 3 644534_1]
te abruvan mahat vai idam sam eva bharāma iti | [JB, 1, 3 644535_1]
tam pṛṣṭhyam ṣaḍaham abhisamabharan | [JB, 1, 3 644536_1]
te abruvan mahat vai idam sam eva bharāma iti | [JB, 1, 3 644537_1]
{JB, 1, 4}
tam trirātram tam dvirātram tam aptoryāmam tam atirātram tam vājapeyam tam ṣoḍaśinam tam ukthyam tam agniṣṭomam tam iṣṭi paśubandhān tam cāturmāsyāni tam darśapūrṇamāsau | [JB, 1, 4 644538_1]
tam ete agnihotra āhutī abhisamabharan | [JB, 1, 4 644538_2]
saḥ atas na parājayata | [JB, 1, 4 644539_1]
etat vai aparājitam yat agnihotram | [JB, 1, 4 644540_1]
na ha vai parājayate yaḥ evam veda | [JB, 1, 4 644541_1]
agniḥ jyotiḥ jyotiḥ agniḥ svāhā iti aṣṭa akṣareṇa juhoti | [JB, 1, 4 644543_1]
aṣṭa akṣarā gāyatrī | [JB, 1, 4 644544_1]
tat eva prātassavanam | [JB, 1, 4 644545_1]
manasā niṣkevalyena uttarām āhutim juhoti | [JB, 1, 4 644546_1]
tat eva mādhyaṃdinam savanam | [JB, 1, 4 644547_1]
upamṛṣṭe prāśnāti | [JB, 1, 4 644548_1]
tat eva tṛtīyasavanam | [JB, 1, 4 644549_1]
lelihitam iva hi tat tṛtīyasavanam | [JB, 1, 4 644550_1]
upariṣṭāt apaḥ upaspṛśati | [JB, 1, 4 644551_1]
avabhṛthaḥ eva asya sa | [JB, 1, 4 644552_1]
sa yat ete sāyamāhutī juhoti etābhyām eva asya āhutibhyām sarvaiḥ etaiḥ yajña kratubhiḥ iṣṭam bhavati | [JB, 1, 4 644553_1]
atha yat ete prātarāhutī juhoti etābhyām eva asya āhutibhyām sarvaiḥ etaiḥ yajña kratubhiḥ iṣṭam bhavati | [JB, 1, 4 644554_1]
tat etat aparyantam yat agnihotram | [JB, 1, 4 644555_1]
{JB, 1, 5}
atha paśu kāmaḥ sāyam paśuṣu sameteṣu agnihotram juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 5 644556_1]
brahma vai agnihotram | [JB, 1, 5 644557_1]
brahmaṇā eva etat paśūn parigṛhṇāti | [JB, 1, 5 644558_1]
avisṛṣṭeṣu prātar | [JB, 1, 5 644559_1]
brahma vai agnihotram | [JB, 1, 5 644560_1]
brahmaṇā eva etat paśūn parigṛhṇāti | [JB, 1, 5 644561_1]
saḥ etān brahmaṇā ubhayatas paśūn parigṛhṇīte | [JB, 1, 5 644562_1]
ava paśūn runddhe | [JB, 1, 5 644563_1]
bahu paśuḥ bhavati | [JB, 1, 5 644564_1]
atha svarga kāmaḥ dvau samudrau a caryau vitatau mahāntau āvarīvartete pathā iva padau iti | [JB, 1, 5 644565_1]
dvau ha eva samudrau a caryau ahar ca eva rātriḥ ca | [JB, 1, 5 644567_1]
te ye naktam juhvati rātrim eva te samudram praviśanti | [JB, 1, 5 644568_1]
atha ye udite juhvati ahar eva te samudram praviśanti | [JB, 1, 5 644569_1]
tayoḥ vai etayoḥ atyayanam asti yathā vaiṣacam vā syāt setoḥ vā saṃkramaṇam astamite purā tamisrāyai su vyuṣṭāyām purā udayāt | [JB, 1, 5 644570_1]
{JB, 1, 6}
atha u ha etau śyāma śabalau eva yat ahar rātre | [JB, 1, 6 644571_1]
ahar vai śabalaḥ | [JB, 1, 6 644572_1]
rātriḥ śyāmaḥ | [JB, 1, 6 644572_2]
te ye naktam juhvati rātrim eva te śyāmam praviśanti | [JB, 1, 6 644573_1]
atha ye udite juhvati ahar eva te śabalam praviśanti | [JB, 1, 6 644574_1]

atha u ha eṣu savitā eva dyumnaḥ | [JB, 1, 6 644576_1]
savitā vai prajāpatiḥ | [JB, 1, 6 644577_1]
prajāpatiḥ viśve devāḥ | [JB, 1, 6 644578_1]
prajāpatau eva asya tat viśveṣu deveṣu hutam bhavati | [JB, 1, 6 644579_1]
tat etat prājāpatyam yat agnihotram | [JB, 1, 6 644580_1]
atha yat etat prātar prabhāti etasmin vai dyumne prajāpatiḥ prajāḥ prajanayāṃcakāra | [JB, 1, 6 644581_1]
savitā vai prajāpatiḥ | [JB, 1, 6 644582_1]
prajāpatiḥ viśve devāḥ | [JB, 1, 6 644583_1]
prajāpatau eva asya tat viśveṣu deveṣu hutam bhavati | [JB, 1, 6 644584_1]
tat etat vaiśvadevam yat agnihotram | [JB, 1, 6 644585_1]

annam vai agnihotram | [JB, 1, 6 644587_1]
annādyam eva etat ahar rātrayoḥ mukhataḥ apidadhāti | [JB, 1, 6 644588_1]
evam eva punar prātar saṃdhattaḥ | [JB, 1, 6 644589_1]
annam vai agnihotram | [JB, 1, 6 644590_1]

{JB, 1, 7}
asau vai ādityaḥ astam yan ṣoḍhā vimrocati | [JB, 1, 7 644592_1]
vyamrucat iti ha sma vai etam pūrve purāṇinaḥ ācakṣate | [JB, 1, 7 644593_1]
atha etarhi nyamrucat iti | [JB, 1, 7 644594_1]
sa vai eṣaḥ astam yan brāhmaṇam eva śraddhayā praviśati payasā paśūn tejasā agnim ūrjā oṣadhīḥ rasena apaḥ svadhayā vanaspatīn | [JB, 1, 7 644595_1]
sa yat brāhmaṇaḥ agnihotra pātrāṇi nirṇenekti yat pariceṣṭati yayā eva enam śraddhayā praviṣṭaḥ bhavati tām eva asmin tat saṃbharati | [JB, 1, 7 644596_1]
atha yat payaḥ duhanti yena payasā paśūn praviṣṭaḥ bhavati tat eva asmin tat saṃbharati | [JB, 1, 7 644597_1]
atha yat aṅgārān nirūhati yena tejasā agnim praviṣṭaḥ bhavati tat eva asmin tat saṃbharati | [JB, 1, 7 644598_1]
atha yat tṛṇena avadyotayati yayā ūrjā oṣadhīḥ praviṣṭaḥ bhavati tām eva asmin tat saṃbharati | [JB, 1, 7 644599_1]
atha yat apaḥ pratyānayati yena rasena apaḥ praviṣṭaḥ bhavati tam eva asmin tat saṃbharati | [JB, 1, 7 644600_1]
atha yat samidham abhyādadhāti yayā svadhayā vanaspatīn praviṣṭaḥ bhavati tām eva asmin tat saṃbharati | [JB, 1, 7 644601_1]
{JB, 1, 8}
tam evam saṃbhṛtya sāyam juhoti | [JB, 1, 8 644602_1]
sa tām garbha kṛtaḥ rātrim vasati | [JB, 1, 8 644603_1]
evam eva punar saṃbhṛtya prātar juhoti | [JB, 1, 8 644604_1]
tam janayati | [JB, 1, 8 644605_1]
saḥ asya jāyamānaḥ eva sarvam pāpmānam apahanti | [JB, 1, 8 644606_1]
devāḥ vai prajāpateḥ ajāyanta | [JB, 1, 8 644607_1]
eṣaḥ u evaṃvidaḥ jāyate | [JB, 1, 8 644608_1]
sa yāvantam prajāpatiḥ lokam ajayat tāvantam jayati | [JB, 1, 8 644609_1]
atha u ha īkṣate ayam vāva mām anuṣṭhyā saṃbharati hanta ayam sa aṅgaḥ sa tanuḥ a vihrutaḥ jarasam gacchatu iti | [JB, 1, 8 644610_1]
sa ha sa aṅgaḥ eva sa tanuḥ a vihrutaḥ jarasam gacchati | [JB, 1, 8 644611_1]
atha u ha īkṣate ayam vāva mām anuṣṭhyā veda hanta imam eva āviśāni iti | [JB, 1, 8 644612_1]
sa ha evaṃvidam eva āviśati | [JB, 1, 8 644613_1]
saḥ eṣa vai ekaḥ vīraḥ yaḥ eṣa tapati | [JB, 1, 8 644614_1]
eṣaḥ indraḥ | [JB, 1, 8 644614_2]
eṣa prajāpatiḥ | [JB, 1, 8 644614_3]
etasmin ha asya tat hutam bhavati yaḥ evam vidvān agnihotram juhoti | [JB, 1, 8 644615_1]
{JB, 1, 9}
yat ha vai ahnā pāpam kriyate ādityaḥ tat kārayati yat rātryā agniḥ tat | [JB, 1, 9 644616_1]
tau abrūtām ittham ced vai bhaviṣyāvaḥ na vai tarhi śakṣyāvaḥ prajāḥ bhartum hanta annam eva asāva anyonyasmin eva ātmānam juhavāva iti | [JB, 1, 9 644618_1]
sa yat ādityaḥ astam eti agnau eva tat ātmānam juhoti | [JB, 1, 9 644619_1]

ādityam udyantam agniḥ anūdeti | [JB, 1, 9 644621_1]
āditye eva tat ātmānam juhoti | [JB, 1, 9 644622_1]
sa yat kim ca agniḥ rātryā pāpam karoti tat asya ādityaḥ ahnā apahanti | [JB, 1, 9 644623_1]
sa yathā ahiḥ ahi chavyai nirmucyeta yathā muñjāt iṣīkām vivṛhet evam eva sarvasmāt pāpmanaḥ nirmucyete sa yaḥ evam vidvān agnihotram juhoti | [JB, 1, 9 644624_1]
{JB, 1, 10}

sa yathā ahiḥ ahi chavyai nirmucyeta yathā muñjāt iṣīkām vivṛhet evam eva sarvasmāt pāpmanaḥ nirmucyate | [JB, 1, 10 644627_1]
tat yathā hiraṇye dhmāte na kaścana nyaṅgaḥ pāpmā pariśiṣyate evam ha eva asmin na kaścana nyaṅgaḥ pāpmā pariśiṣyate yaḥ evam vidvān agnihotram juhoti | [JB, 1, 10 644628_1]
{JB, 1, 11}
atha ha sma āha nagarī jānaśruteyaḥ asau vai ādityaḥ astam yan agnim eva yonim praviśati iti | [JB, 1, 11 644629_1]
sa yat ete sāyamāhutī juhoti etasya eva tat ādityasya pṛṣṭhe pratitiṣṭhati | [JB, 1, 11 644630_1]
yathā ubhaya padī pratitiṣṭhet tādṛś tat | [JB, 1, 11 644630_2]
tat | [JB, 1, 11 644630_3]
atha yat ete prātarāhutī juhoti utthāpayati eva enam tābhyām | [JB, 1, 11 644631_1]
sa yathā hastī hasti āsanam upari āsīnam ādāya uttiṣṭhet evam eva eṣā devatā etat vidvāṃsam juhvatam ādāya udeti | [JB, 1, 11 644632_1]
sā enam tam lokam gamayati yaḥ etasyai yatas param na asti | [JB, 1, 11 644633_1]
sa yat kim ca parācīnam ādityāt tat amṛtam | [JB, 1, 11 644634_1]
tat abhijayati | [JB, 1, 11 644634_2]
atha yat arvācīnam ādityāt ahorātre tat upamathnītaḥ yathā reṣmā upamathnīyāt evam | [JB, 1, 11 644635_1]
bahavaḥ ha vai ādityāt parāñcaḥ lokāḥ | [JB, 1, 11 644636_1]
te asya sarve āptāḥ bhavanti te jitāḥ teṣu asya sarveṣu kāma cāraḥ bhavati yaḥ evam vidvān agnihotram juhoti | [JB, 1, 11 644637_1]
{JB, 1, 12}
devāḥ vai mṛtyunā samayatanta | [JB, 1, 12 644639_1]
sa yaḥ ha sa mṛtyuḥ agniḥ eva sa | [JB, 1, 12 644640_1]
te abruvan eta imam jigīṣāma iti | [JB, 1, 12 644641_1]
te abruvan ājya āhutim juhavāma tayā enam jigīṣāma iti | [JB, 1, 12 644642_1]
tathā iti | [JB, 1, 12 644643_1]
te ājya āhutim ajuhavuḥ | [JB, 1, 12 644644_1]
tām annam akuruta | [JB, 1, 12 644645_1]
tām pratyudadīpyata | [JB, 1, 12 644645_2]
tasmāt yatra ājya āhutim juhvati pratyuddīpyate eva | [JB, 1, 12 644646_1]

tathā iti | [JB, 1, 12 644648_1]
te paśum ālabhya medaḥ samavadāya paśu āhutim ajuhavuḥ | [JB, 1, 12 644649_1]
tām annam akuruta | [JB, 1, 12 644650_1]

tathā iti | [JB, 1, 12 644653_1]
te kṣīra āhutim ajuhavuḥ | [JB, 1, 12 644654_1]
tayā enam ajayan | [JB, 1, 12 644655_1]

te abruvan ajeṣma vai enam annena hanta anapajayyam jigīṣāma iti | [JB, 1, 12 644657_1]
{JB, 1, 13}
te abruvan soma āhutim juhavāma tayā enam jigīṣāma iti | [JB, 1, 13 644658_1]
tathā iti | [JB, 1, 13 644659_1]
te somena ayajanta | [JB, 1, 13 644660_1]
te soma āhutim ajuhavuḥ | [JB, 1, 13 644661_1]
tayā enam prājayan | [JB, 1, 13 644662_1]

atha yat kṣīra āhutim juhoti jayati eva enam tena | [JB, 1, 13 644665_1]

{JB, 1, 14}
prāṇāya tvā iti samidham abhyādadhāti | [JB, 1, 14 644668_1]
apāne amṛtam adhām svāhā iti juhoti | [JB, 1, 14 644669_1]
atha srucam abhimṛśati hṛdayam pretiḥ manaḥ saṃtatiḥ cakṣuḥ ānatiḥ śrotram upanatiḥ vāc āgatiḥ pratītam devebhyaḥ juṣṭam havyam asthāt amṛte mām adhāt ā mām prāṇāḥ viśantu bhūyase sukṛtāya iti | [JB, 1, 14 644670_1]
sa ha bhūyaḥ eva sukṛtam karoti | [JB, 1, 14 644674_1]
atha u ha enam amuṣmin loke na pāpī vāc āgacchati yaḥ evam vidvān agnihotram juhoti | [JB, 1, 14 644675_1]
{JB, 1, 15}
tat āhuḥ yat jīvan puruṣaḥ karoti eva sādhu karoti pāpam kā tayoḥ duṣkṛta sukṛtayoḥ vyāvṛttiḥ iti | [JB, 1, 15 644676_1]
yat ha vai jīvan puruṣaḥ sādhu karoti prāṇān tat abhisaṃpadyate | [JB, 1, 15 644677_1]
atha yat duṣkṛtam śarīram tat | [JB, 1, 15 644678_1]
sa yat asmāt lokāt evaṃvid praiti tasya prāṇena saha sukṛtam utkrāmati śarīreṇa saha duṣkṛtam hīyate | [JB, 1, 15 644679_1]
tat āhuḥ durviditam vai tat yadā martyavān duṣkṛtena saha vasāt yaḥ vai etena jīvan eva vyāvartate tat su viditam iti | [JB, 1, 15 644680_1]
tat vai etat agnihotram eva abhisaṃpadyate | [JB, 1, 15 644682_1]
{JB, 1, 16}
manaḥ vai anu prāṇāḥ | [JB, 1, 16 644683_1]
vācam anu ātmā | [JB, 1, 16 644683_2]
sa yat vācā pūrvām āhutim juhoti manasā uttarām tat duṣkṛta sukṛte vyāvartayati | [JB, 1, 16 644684_1]
tasmāt āhuḥ na ete āhutī saṃsṛjye duṣkṛta sukṛte hi etābhyām vyāvartayati iti | [JB, 1, 16 644685_1]
sa yat sāyamāhutyoḥ vācā pūrvām āhutim juhoti yat eva ahnā pāpam karoti tasmāt eva tayā vyāvartate | [JB, 1, 16 644687_1]
atha yat manasā uttarām yat eva rātryā pāpam karoti tasmāt eva tayā vyāvartate | [JB, 1, 16 644688_1]
atha yat prātarāhutyoḥ vācā pūrvām āhutim juhoti yat eva rātryā pāpam karoti tasmāt eva tayā vyāvartate | [JB, 1, 16 644689_1]
atha yat manasā uttarām yat eva ahnā pāpam karoti tasmāt eva tayā vyāvartate | [JB, 1, 16 644690_1]
{JB, 1, 17}
dve ha vāva yonī | [JB, 1, 17 644692_1]
deva yoniḥ ha eva anyā manuṣya yoniḥ anyā | [JB, 1, 17 644693_1]
dvau u ha eva lokau | [JB, 1, 17 644694_1]
deva lokaḥ ha eva anyaḥ manuṣya lokaḥ anyaḥ | [JB, 1, 17 644695_1]
sā yā manuṣya yoniḥ manuṣya loke eva sa | [JB, 1, 17 644696_1]
tat striyai prajananam | [JB, 1, 17 644697_1]
atas adhi prajāḥ prajāyante | [JB, 1, 17 644698_1]
tasmāt u kalyāṇīm jāyām iccheta kalyāṇe me ātmā saṃbhavāt iti | [JB, 1, 17 644699_1]
tasmāt u jāyām jugupset na id mama yonau mama loke anyaḥ saṃbhavāt iti | [JB, 1, 17 644700_1]
tasya vai sambhaviṣyataḥ prāṇāḥ agre praviśanti atha retaḥ sicyate | [JB, 1, 17 644701_1]
saḥ imān prāṇān ākāśān abhinirvartate | [JB, 1, 17 644702_1]
tasmāt u samānasya eva retasaḥ sataḥ yādṛśaḥ eva bhavati tādṛśaḥ jāyate | [JB, 1, 17 644703_1]
atha eṣā deva yoniḥ deva lokaḥ yat āhavanīyaḥ | [JB, 1, 17 644704_1]
eṣā ha vai deva yoniḥ deva lokaḥ | [JB, 1, 17 644705_1]
tasmāt yaḥ gārhapatye juhuyāt akṛtam karoti iti eva enam manyeran | [JB, 1, 17 644706_1]
sa yat juhoti yaḥ sādhu karoti etasyām eva enat deva yonau ātmānam siñcati | [JB, 1, 17 644707_1]
saḥ asya ātmā amuṣmin āditye sambhavati | [JB, 1, 17 644708_1]
sa ha evam vidvān dvi ātmā dvi yoniḥ | [JB, 1, 17 644709_1]
eka ātmā ha eva eka yoniḥ etat a vidvān | [JB, 1, 17 644710_1]
sa yad asmāl lokād evaṃvit praiti | [JB, 1, 17 20]
{JB, 1, 18}
tasya prāṇaḥ prathamaḥ utkrāmati | [JB, 1, 18 644712_1]
sa ha iyattām devebhyaḥ ācaṣṭe iyat asya sādhu kṛtam iyat pāpam iti | [JB, 1, 18 644713_1]
atha ha ayam dhūmena saha ūrdhvaḥ utkrāmati | [JB, 1, 18 644714_1]
tasya ha etasya ṛtavaḥ dvārapāḥ | [JB, 1, 18 644715_1]
tebhyaḥ ha etena prabruvīta | [JB, 1, 18 644716_1]
vicakṣaṇād ṛtavo reta ābhṛtam ardhamāsyaṃ prasutāt pitryāvatas taṃ mā puṃsi kartary erayadhvaṃ puṃsaḥ kartur mātary āsiṣikta | [JB, 1, 18 3.2]
sa upajāyopajāyamāno dvādaśena trayodaśopamāsaḥ saṃ tad vide prati tad vide 'haṃ taṃ mā ṛtavo 'mṛta ānayadhvam iti | [JB, 1, 18 4.1]
tam ha ṛtavaḥ ānayante | [JB, 1, 18 644719_1]
yathā vidvān vidvāṃsam yathā jānan jānantam evam ha enam ṛtavaḥ ānayante | [JB, 1, 18 644720_1]
tam ha atyarjayante | [JB, 1, 18 644721_1]
sa ha etam āgacchati tapantam | [JB, 1, 18 644722_1]
tam ha āgatam pṛcchati kaḥ tvam asi iti | [JB, 1, 18 644723_1]
sa yaḥ ha nāmnā vā gotreṇa vā prabrūte tam ha āha yaḥ te ayam mayi ātmā abhūt eṣa te saḥ iti | [JB, 1, 18 644724_1]
tasmin ha ātman pratipatte ṛtavaḥ saṃpalāyya pad gṛhītam apakarṣanti | [JB, 1, 18 644725_1]
tasya ha ahorātre lokam āpnutaḥ | [JB, 1, 18 644726_1]
tasmai u ha etena prabruvīta kaḥ aham asmi suvar tvam sa tvām svargyam svar agām iti | [JB, 1, 18 644727_1]
kaḥ ha vai prajāpatiḥ | [JB, 1, 18 644729_1]
atha ha evaṃvid eva suvargaḥ | [JB, 1, 18 644730_1]
sa hi suvar gacchati | [JB, 1, 18 644731_1]
tam ha āha yaḥ tvam asi saḥ aham asmi yaḥ aham asmi sa tvam asi ehi iti | [JB, 1, 18 644732_1]
saḥ etam eva su kṛta rasam apyeti | [JB, 1, 18 644734_1]
tasya putrāḥ dāyam upayanti pitaraḥ sādhu kṛtyām | [JB, 1, 18 644735_1]
sa ha evam vidvān dvi ātmā dvi dāyaḥ | [JB, 1, 18 644736_1]
eka ātmā ha eva eka dāyaḥ etat a vidvān agnihotram juhoti | [JB, 1, 18 644737_1]
{JB, 1, 19}
vāc vai agnihotrī | [JB, 1, 19 644738_1]
tasyai manaḥ eva vatsaḥ | [JB, 1, 19 644739_1]
manasā vai vācam prattām duhre | [JB, 1, 19 644740_1]
vatsena vai mātaram prattām duhre | [JB, 1, 19 644741_1]
tat vai idam manaḥ pūrvam yat paścāt vāc anveti | [JB, 1, 19 644742_1]
tasmāt vatsam pūrvam yantam paścāt mātā anveti | [JB, 1, 19 644743_1]
hṛdayam eva methī upadohanī | [JB, 1, 19 644744_1]
prāṇaḥ rajjuḥ | [JB, 1, 19 644744_2]
prāṇena eva vāc ca manaḥ ca abhihite | [JB, 1, 19 644745_1]
rajjvā vai vatsam ca mātaram ca abhidadhāti | [JB, 1, 19 644746_1]
tat ha janakaḥ vaidehaḥ yājñavalkyam papraccha vettha agnihotram yājñavalkya iti | [JB, 1, 19 644747_1]
veda iti ha uvāca | [JB, 1, 19 644748_1]
kim iti | [JB, 1, 19 644749_1]
payaḥ iti | [JB, 1, 19 644750_1]
yat payaḥ na syāt kena juhuyāḥ iti | [JB, 1, 19 644751_1]
vrīhi yavābhyām iti | [JB, 1, 19 644752_1]
yat vrīhi yavau na syātām kena juhuyāḥ iti | [JB, 1, 19 644753_1]
yat anyat dhānyam tena iti | [JB, 1, 19 644754_1]
yat anyat dhānyam na syāt kena juhuyāḥ iti | [JB, 1, 19 644755_1]
āraṇyābhiḥ oṣadhībhiḥ iti | [JB, 1, 19 644756_1]
yat āraṇyāḥ oṣadhayaḥ na syuḥ kena juhuyāḥ iti | [JB, 1, 19 644757_1]
adbhiḥ iti | [JB, 1, 19 644758_1]
yat āpaḥ na syuḥ kena juhuyāḥ iti | [JB, 1, 19 644759_1]
sa ha uvāca na vai iha tarhi kiṃcana āsīt atha etat u hūyate iva satyam śraddhāyām iti | [JB, 1, 19 644760_1]
tam ha uvāca vettha agnihotram yājñavalkya namaḥ te astu sahasram bhagavaḥ dadmaḥ iti | [JB, 1, 19 644761_1]
atha ha enam upajagau | [JB, 1, 19 644762_1]
{JB, 1, 20}
kim nu vidvān pravasati agnihotrī gṛhebhyaḥ kathā tat asya kāvyam kathā saṃtataḥ agnibhiḥ iti | [JB, 1, 20 644763_1]
yat agnīn ādhāya atha apapravasati katham asya an apaproṣitam bhavati iti | [JB, 1, 20 644764_1]
sa ha uvāca vājasaneyaḥ yaḥ javiṣṭhaḥ bhuvaneṣu sa vidvān pravasan vide tathā tat asya kāvyam tathā saṃtataḥ agnibhiḥ iti | [JB, 1, 20 644765_1]
manaḥ iti ha uvāca | [JB, 1, 20 644767_1]
manaḥ vāva bhuvaneṣu javiṣṭham | [JB, 1, 20 644768_1]
manasā eva asya an apaproṣitam bhavati iti ha tat uvāca | [JB, 1, 20 644769_1]
atha ha enam upajagau | [JB, 1, 20 644770_1]
yat sa dūraṃ paretyātha tatra pramādyati kasmin sāsya hutāhutir gṛhe yām asya juhvatīti | [JB, 1, 20 9]
sa ha uvāca vājasaneyaḥ | [JB, 1, 20 644772_1]
yo jāgāra bhuvaneṣu sa vidvān pravasan vide tasmin sāsya hutāhutir gṛhe yām asya juhvatīti | [JB, 1, 20 11]
prāṇaḥ iti ha uvāca | [JB, 1, 20 644774_1]
prāṇaḥ vāva bhuvaneṣu jāgaraḥ | [JB, 1, 20 644775_1]
prāṇe eva asya sā hutā āhutiḥ bhavati | [JB, 1, 20 644776_1]
tasmāt āhuḥ prāṇaḥ agnihotram iti | [JB, 1, 20 644777_1]
yāvat hi eva prāṇena prāṇiti tāvat agnihotram juhoti | [JB, 1, 20 644778_1]
{JB, 1, 21}
raudraṃ gavi vāyavyam upasṛṣṭam āśvinaṃ duhyamānam agnīṣomīyaṃ dugdhaṃ vāruṇam adhiśritaṃ vaiśvadevā bindavaḥ pauṣṇam udantaṃ sārasvataṃ viṣyandamānaṃ maitraṃ śaro dhātur udvāsitaṃ bṛhaspater unnītaṃ savituḥ prakrāntaṃ dyāvāpṛthivyor hriyamāṇam indrāgnyor upasannam agneḥ pūrvāhutiḥ prajāpater uttaraindraṃ hutam | [JB, 1, 21 1]
tad etat saptadaśam agnihotram | [JB, 1, 21 2]
saptadaśa u eva vājapeyaḥ | [JB, 1, 21 3]
sa ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoty ubhāv eva lokāv abhijayati yaś cāgnihotrahuto yaś ca vājapeyayājinaḥ | [JB, 1, 21 4]
trayo 'gnihotre sthāṇava iti ha smāha śāṇḍilyaḥ | [JB, 1, 21 5]
yad apradīptāyāṃ samidhi juhoti sa sthāṇuḥ | [JB, 1, 21 6]
yad enām aparādhnoti sa sthāṇuḥ | [JB, 1, 21 7]
yad ene saṃsṛjati sa sthāṇuḥ | [JB, 1, 21 8]
ādīptāyai samidhaḥ samunmukhe juhoti | [JB, 1, 21 9]
atihāyottarām āhutiṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 21 10]
pra ha saptadaśa saptadaśa sahasrapoṣān puṣyati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 21 11]
{JB, 1, 22}
āruṇir vājasaneyo prakur vārṣṇaḥ priyo jānaśruteyo buḍila āśvatarāśvir vaiyāghrapadya ity ete ha pañca mahābrahmā āsuḥ | [JB, 1, 22 1]
te hocur janako vā ayaṃ vaideho 'gnihotre 'nuśiṣṭaḥ sa no 'tivadann iva manyata eta tam agnihotre kathāṃ vādayiṣyāma iti | [JB, 1, 22 2]
te hājagmuḥ | [JB, 1, 22 3]
te ha brahmacāriṇam ūcuḥ pra ṇo brūhīti | [JB, 1, 22 4]
tān ha provāca | [JB, 1, 22 5]
tebhyo ha proktebhyaḥ pṛthag āsanāni pṛthag udakāni pṛthaṅ madhuparkān pṛthag āvasathān pṛthak pañcabhyaḥ pañcāpacitīś cakāra | [JB, 1, 22 6]
atha haiṣāṃ sabhāga āvavrājoptvā keśaśmaśrūṇi nakhān nikṛtyājyābhyajya daṇḍopānahaṃ bibhrat | [JB, 1, 22 7]
tān hovāca brāhmaṇāḥ kathā bhagavanto no 'nusaṃvādayatheti | [JB, 1, 22 8]
ati no 'vādīr iti hocuḥ | [JB, 1, 22 9]
atha hainān pūrvaḥ papraccha brāhmaṇāḥ kathā bhagavanto yūyam agnihotraṃ juhutheti | [JB, 1, 22 10]
ati vai no 'vādīr iti hocur yo no bhūyasaḥ sataḥ pūrvo 'prākṣīr gautama pratibrūhīti | [JB, 1, 22 11]
{JB, 1, 23}
sa hovāca yaśa ity eva samrāḍ aham agnihotraṃ juhomi tasmād ahaṃ yaśo 'smi yaśo vāva me prajāyām antato bhaviteti | [JB, 1, 23 1]
taṃ hovāca gautama kiṃ yaśa iti | [JB, 1, 23 2]
agnim upadiśann uvācedaṃ yaśa ity ado yaśa ity ādityaṃ so 'ham ado yaśo 'smin yaśasi sāyaṃ juhomīdaṃ yaśo 'muṣmin yaśasi prātar juhomyetāveva mā tad gamayiṣyato yatra sarve kāmā etau me punarmṛtyum apajeṣyata iti | [JB, 1, 23 3]
suhutaṃ devān rādhayānīti ha praśaśaṃsa | [JB, 1, 23 4]
atha hāparaṃ papraccha kathā bhagavas tvam agnihotraṃ juhoṣīti | [JB, 1, 23 5]
sa hovāca vājasaneyaḥ satyam ity eva samrāḍ aham agnihotraṃ juhomi tasmād ahaṃ satyam asmi tasmān mama satyam iva vadataḥ prakāśa iti | [JB, 1, 23 6]
taṃ hovāca yājñavalkyaḥ kiṃ satyam iti | [JB, 1, 23 7]
agnim upadiśann uvācedaṃ satyam ity adaḥ satyam ity ādityaṃ so 'ham adaḥ satyam asmin satye sāyaṃ juhomīdaṃ satyam amuṣmin satye prātar juhomyetāveva mā tad gamayiṣyato yatra sarve kāmā etau me punarmṛtyum apajeṣyata iti | [JB, 1, 23 8]
suhutaṃ devān rādhayānīti haiva praśaśaṃsa | [JB, 1, 23 9]
atha hāparaṃ papraccha kathā bhagavas tvam agnihotraṃ juhoṣīti | [JB, 1, 23 10]
{JB, 1, 24}
sa hovāca prakur vārṣṇo bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vittānām ity eva samrāḍ aham agnihotraṃ juhomi tasmād ahaṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vittānām asmi bhūyiṣṭhaṃ vāva me śreṣṭhaṃ vittānāṃ prajāyām antato bhaviteti | [JB, 1, 24 1]
taṃ hovācāgniveśya kiṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vittānām iti | [JB, 1, 24 2]
agnim upadiśann uvācedaṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vittānām ity ado bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vittānām ity ādityaṃ so 'ham ado bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vittānām asmin bhūyiṣṭhe śreṣṭhe vittānāṃ sāyaṃ juhomīdaṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vittānām amuṣmin bhūyiṣṭhe śreṣṭhe vittānāṃ prātar juhomy etāv eva mā tad gamayiṣyato yatra sarve kāmā etau me punarmṛtyum apajeṣyata iti | [JB, 1, 24 3]
suhutaṃ devān rādhayānīti haiva praśaśaṃsa | [JB, 1, 24 4]
atha hāparaṃ papraccha kathā bhagavas tvam agnihotraṃ juhoṣīti | [JB, 1, 24 5]
sa hovāca priyo jānaśruteyas teja ity eva samrāḍ aham agnihotraṃ juhomi tasmād ahaṃ tejo 'smi tejo vāva me prajāyām antato bhaviteti | [JB, 1, 24 6]
taṃ hovāca kāṇḍvīya kiṃ teja iti | [JB, 1, 24 7]
agnim upadiśann uvācedaṃ teja ity adas teja ity ādityaṃ so 'ham adas tejo 'smiṃs tejasi sāyaṃ juhomīdaṃ tejo 'muṣmiṃs tejasi prātar juhomy etāv eva mā tad gamayiṣyato yatra sarve kāmā etau me punarmṛtyum apajeṣyata iti | [JB, 1, 24 8]
suhutaṃ devān rādhayāni iti haiva praśaśaṃsa | [JB, 1, 24 9]
atha hāparaṃ papraccha kathā bhagavas tvam agnihotraṃ juhoṣīti | [JB, 1, 24 10]
{JB, 1, 25}
sa hovāca buḍila āśvatarāśvir vaiyāghrapadyo 'rkāśvamedhāvity eva samrāḍ aham agnihotraṃ juhomy annaṃ hy etad devānāṃ yad arko 'śvo medho medhya iti | [JB, 1, 25 1]
taṃ hovāca vaiyāghrapadya ko 'rkaḥ ko 'śvo medho medhya iti | [JB, 1, 25 2]
agnim upadiśann uvācāyam arka ityasāvaśvo medho medhya ity ādityaṃ so 'ham amum aśvaṃ medhaṃ medhyam asminn arke sāyaṃ juhomīmam arkam amuṣminn aśve medhe medhye prātar juhomy etāveva mā tad gamayiṣyato yatra sarve kāmā etau me punarmṛtyum apajeṣyata iti | [JB, 1, 25 3]
suhutam iti ha praśasyovāca yo ha kila mahyam agnihotra itiṃ ca gatiṃ ca brūyāt tasmā ahaṃ varaṃ dadyām iti | [JB, 1, 25 4]
te hocur na nvai vayam agnihotra itiṃ ca gatiṃ cānūcimahe tvam asmabhyam agnihotra itiṃ ca gatiṃ ca brūhi vayaṃ tubhyaṃ pṛthak pañca varān dadma iti | [JB, 1, 25 5]
agnim upadiśann uvāceyam itir ity asau gatir ity ādityaṃ so 'ham amūṃ gatim asyām itau sāyaṃ juhomīmām itim amuṣyāṃ gatau prātar juhomy etāv eva mā tad gamayiṣyato yatra sarve kāmā etau me punarmṛtyum apajeṣyata iti | [JB, 1, 25 6]
suhutam iti ha praśasyocur varān vṛṇīṣva yān adāmeti | [JB, 1, 25 7]
sa hovācaiṣa eva me varo 'ham eva yuṣmabhyaṃ pṛthak pañca sahasrāṇi śatāśvāni dadānīti | [JB, 1, 25 8]
etāni vā agnihotra upāsanāny ete kāmāḥ | [JB, 1, 25 9]
etān eva kāmān avarunddhe ya evaṃ vedātho yasyaivaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 25 10]
{JB, 1, 26}
agnīn ādadhānaḥ prātar evoddharet | [JB, 1, 26 1]
tad dviḥ sāyaṃ dviḥ prātar juhoti | [JB, 1, 26 2]
catasra āhutayaḥ sampadyante | [JB, 1, 26 3]
catuṣpadā vai paśavo ye ca grāmyā ye cāraṇyāḥ | [JB, 1, 26 4]
teṣām evaitat pratyāśaṃ pratyapacayati | [JB, 1, 26 5]
eṣa vai mṛtyur yad agnī rihann eva nāma | [JB, 1, 26 6]
tam eva tābhir āhutibhiḥ śamayitvā pṛthivīṃ lokānāṃ jayaty agniṃ devaṃ devānām | [JB, 1, 26 7]
agner devasya sāyujyaṃ salokatāṃ samabhyārohati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 26 8]
sa tato dhūmam eva rathaṃ samāsthāya vāyoḥ salokatām abhiprayāti | [JB, 1, 26 9]
dvyahaṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 26 10]
aṣṭāv āhutayaḥ sampadyante | [JB, 1, 26 11]
aṣṭāśaphā ha vai paśavo ye ca grāmyā ye cāraṇyāḥ | [JB, 1, 26 12]
teṣām evaitat pratyāśaṃ pratyapacayati | [JB, 1, 26 13]
eṣa vai mṛtyur yad vāyur ajira eva nāma | [JB, 1, 26 14]
tam eva tābhir āhutibhiḥ śamayitvāntarikṣaṃ lokānāṃ jayati vāyuṃ devaṃ devānām | [JB, 1, 26 15]
vāyor devasya sāyujyaṃ salokatāṃ samabhyārohati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 26 16]
{JB, 1, 27}
sa tato reṣmāṇam eva rathaṃ samāsthāyādityasya salokatām abhiprayāti | [JB, 1, 27 1]
tryahaṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 27 2]
dvādaśāhutayaḥ sampadyante | [JB, 1, 27 3]
dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ | [JB, 1, 27 4]
saṃvatsaro vā idaṃ sarvaṃ | [JB, 1, 27 5]
sa yad ihāśnāti yat pibati yasmai kasmaicana prativyādadāti sarvaṃ tad asyānaśitaṃ bhavati yāvajjīvānāśakavratī bhavati | [JB, 1, 27 6]
eṣa vai mṛtyur yad ādityo mrocann eva nāma | [JB, 1, 27 7]
tam eva tābhir āhutibhiḥ śamayitvā divaṃ lokānāṃ jayaty ādityaṃ devaṃ devānām | [JB, 1, 27 8]
ādityasya devasya sāyujyaṃ salokatāṃ samabhyārohati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 27 9]
{JB, 1, 28}
sa tato raśmīn eva rathaṃ samāsthāya candramasaḥ salokatām abhiprayāti | [JB, 1, 28 1]
caturahaṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 28 2]
ṣoḍaśāhutayaḥ sampadyante | [JB, 1, 28 3]
ṣoḍaśakalaṃ vai brahma | [JB, 1, 28 4]
ṣoḍaśakalā devāḥ | [JB, 1, 28 5]
ṣoḍaśakalam idaṃ sakṛt sarvam | [JB, 1, 28 6]
sa yad iha ripraṃ pāpaṃ karma karoty ekayaiva tataḥ kalayā | [JB, 1, 28 7]
yathā suvarṇaḥ pravṛttas tapyamānaḥ suvarṇatām abhiniṣpadyata evam eva dviṣatsu bhrātṛvyeṣu malaṃ pāpmānaṃ pratyūhya svargaṃ lokam abhipraiti | [JB, 1, 28 8]
eṣa vai śaśo ya eṣo 'ntaś candramasi | [JB, 1, 28 9]
eṣa hīdaṃ sarvaṃ śāsti | [JB, 1, 28 10]
eṣa vai yamo ya eṣo 'ntaś candramasi | [JB, 1, 28 11]
eṣa hīdaṃ sarvaṃ yamayati | [JB, 1, 28 12]
eṣa vai mṛtyur yad yamo 'tsyann eva nāma | [JB, 1, 28 13]
tam eva tābhir āhutibhiḥ śamayitvorjaṃ lokānāṃ jayati yamaṃ devaṃ devānāṃ | [JB, 1, 28 14]
yamasya devasya sāyujyaṃ salokatāṃ samabhyārohati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 28 15]
{JB, 1, 29}
sa tataḥ svadhām eva hiraṇmayīṃ nāvaṃ samāruhya prajāpateḥ salokatām abhiprayāti | [JB, 1, 29 1]
pañcāhaṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 29 2]

saviṃśo vai prajāpatiḥ | [JB, 1, 29 4]

{JB, 1, 30}

{JB, 1, 37}
atra vai brahma na virājaty anātham aparāyaṇam anuttaram | [JB, 1, 37 1]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ dvādaśāhaṃ brahma juhavāṃcakāra | [JB, 1, 37 2]
tad dvādaśāhaṃ hutvā kīrtiṃ yaśaḥ prajātim amṛtaṃ tad udājahāra | [JB, 1, 37 3]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ dvādaśāhaṃ brahma hutvā prajāpataye pratyūhya svargaṃ lokam abhyuccakrāma | [JB, 1, 37 4]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ dvādaśāhaṃ prajāpatir juhavāṃcakāra | [JB, 1, 37 5]
tad dvādaśāhaṃ hutvā prajñāṃ medhāṃ mīmāṃsāṃ tapas tad udājahāra | [JB, 1, 37 6]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ dvādaśāhaṃ prajāpatir hutvā devebhyaś carṣibhyaś ca pratyūhya svargam eva lokam abhyuccakrāma | [JB, 1, 37 7]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ dvādaśāhaṃ devāś carṣayaś ca juhavāṃcakruḥ | [JB, 1, 37 8]
tad dvādaśāhaṃ hutvā pūrvebhyo manuṣyebhyaḥ pratyūhya svargamveva lokam abhyuccakramuḥ | [JB, 1, 37 9]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ dvādaśāhaṃ brahma juhavāṃcakāra dvādaśāhaṃ prajāpatir dvādaśāhaṃ devāścarṣayaśca | [JB, 1, 37 10]
tad dvādaśāhaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ hutvā kāmān nikāmān āpuḥ | [JB, 1, 37 11]
kimu ya enad yāvajjīvaṃ juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 37 12]
{JB, 1, 38}
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ tryaham eva payasā juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 38 1]
tad vā agniṣṭomasya rūpam | [JB, 1, 38 2]
agniṣṭomenaivāsyeṣṭaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 38 3]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ tryaham eva dadhnā juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 38 4]
tad vai vājapeyasya rūpam | [JB, 1, 38 5]
vājapeyenaivāsyeṣṭaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 38 6]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ tryaham evājyena juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 38 7]
tad vā aśvamedhasya rūpam | [JB, 1, 38 8]
aśvamedhenaivāsyeṣṭaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 38 9]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ tryaham evādbhir juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 38 10]
tad vai puruṣamedhasya rūpam | [JB, 1, 38 11]
puruṣamedhenaivāsyeṣṭaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [JB, 1, 38 12]
svayam ahatavāsā yajamāno 'gnihotraṃ juhuyād ajasreṣv agniṣv apravasan | [JB, 1, 38 13]
trayodaśīṃ rātriṃ somena vā paśunā veṣṭvotsṛjeta | [JB, 1, 38 14]
yathā sāvasān kṛtvā prārjayet tādṛk tat | [JB, 1, 38 15]
tad vai tad agnihotraṃ dvādaśāham eva pūrve manuṣyā juhavāṃcakruḥ | [JB, 1, 38 16]
tasmāt teṣāṃ duhe dhenur vahaty anaḍvān ādhānapratihito 'śvo 'śvatara upatiṣṭhaty adhikakṣyo hastī vahati | [JB, 1, 38 17]
{JB, 1, 39}
upasṛjāgnihotrīm ity āha | [JB, 1, 39 1]
upasṛṣṭe dyāvāpṛthivī rudrā upagṛhṇanti vasūnāṃ dugdhaṃ bhūtakṛtaḥ stha nirūḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayam ity aṅgārān nirūhati | [JB, 1, 39 2]
athādhiśrayati vaiśvānarasyādhiśritam asy agnis te tejo mā pratidhākṣīt satyāya tveti | [JB, 1, 39 3]
athāvadyotayati saṃ jyotiṣā jyotir iti | [JB, 1, 39 4]
athāpaḥ pratyānayati yas te apsu rasaḥ praviṣṭas tena saṃpṛcyasveti | [JB, 1, 39 5]
sa yad evāsya tatra diśo grasante tad evāsya tat samanvānayaty antaritaṃ rakṣo 'ntaritā arātaya iti | [JB, 1, 39 6]
triḥ paryagni karoti | [JB, 1, 39 7]
athodvāsayati divaṃ dṛṃhāntarikṣaṃ dṛṃha pṛthivīṃ dṛṃha prajāṃ paśūñ juhvato me dṛṃheti | [JB, 1, 39 8]
bhūtakṛtaḥ stha pratyūḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayam ity aṅgārān pratyūhati | [JB, 1, 39 9]
atha sruvaṃ ca srucaṃ cādāya niṣṭapati pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātaya iti | [JB, 1, 39 10]
atha srucaṃ saṃmārṣṭi sajūr devebhyaḥ sāyaṃyāvabhya iti sāyam | [JB, 1, 39 11]
sajūr devebhyaḥ prātaryāvabhya iti prātaḥ | [JB, 1, 39 12]
suvarṇāṃ tvā suvarṇamayīṃ hiraṇyayaṣṭir asy amṛtapalāśā sroto yajñānām iti | [JB, 1, 39 13]
sroto haiva sa yajñānāṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 39 14]
athāhonneṣyāmīti | [JB, 1, 39 15]
oṃ mām ahaṃ svargaṃ lokam abhīti brūyāt | [JB, 1, 39 16]
{JB, 1, 40}
sa yaṃ prathamaṃ sruvam unnayati tad vai darśapūrṇamāsayo rūpam | [JB, 1, 40 1]
darśapūrṇamāsābhyām evāsyeṣṭaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān prathamaṃ sruvam unnayati | [JB, 1, 40 2]
atha yaṃ dvitīyaṃ sruvam unnayati tad vai cāturmāsyānāṃ rūpam | [JB, 1, 40 3]
cāturmāsyair evāsyeṣṭaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān dvitīyaṃ sruvam unnayati | [JB, 1, 40 4]
atha yaṃ tṛtīyaṃ sruvam unnayati tad vā iṣṭipaśubandhānāṃ rūpam | [JB, 1, 40 5]
iṣṭipaśubandhair evāsyeṣṭaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvāṃs tṛtīyaṃ sruvam unnayati | [JB, 1, 40 6]
atha yaṃ caturthaṃ sruvam unnayati tad vai tryambakavājapeyāśvamedhānāṃ rūpam | [JB, 1, 40 7]
tryambakavājapeyāśvamedhair evāsyeṣṭaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvāṃś caturthaṃ sruvam unnayati | [JB, 1, 40 8]
atha samidham ādāya prāṅ praiti | [JB, 1, 40 9]
puruṣa it samit tam annam inddhe 'nnasya mā tejasā svargaṃ lokaṃ gamaya yatra devānām ṛṣīṇāṃ priyaṃ dhāma tatra ma idam agnihotraṃ gamayeti tūṣṇīm upasādayati | [JB, 1, 40 10]
atha samidham abhyādadhāti svargasya tvā lokasya saṃkramaṇaṃ hiraṇmayaṃ vaṃśaṃ dadhāmi svāheti | [JB, 1, 40 11]
atha juhoti | [JB, 1, 40 12]
sa yāṃ prathamāṃ juhoti devāṃs tayāpnoti | [JB, 1, 40 13]
atha yāṃ dvitīyāṃ juhoty ṛṣīṃs tayāpnoti | [JB, 1, 40 14]
{JB, 1, 41}
atha upamārṣṭi | [JB, 1, 41 645003_1]
sa yat prathamam upamārṣṭi tena gandharva apsarasaḥ prīṇāti | [JB, 1, 41 645004_1]
tam gandharva apsarasaḥ āhuḥ śraddhā te mā vigāt sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ tṛpya svargam lokam āpnuhi iti | [JB, 1, 41 645005_1]
atha yat dvitīyam upamārṣṭi tena grahān ca pitṝn ca prīṇāti | [JB, 1, 41 645006_1]
tam grahāḥ ca pitaraḥ ca āhuḥ śraddhā te mā vigāt sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ tṛpya svargam lokam āpnuhi iti | [JB, 1, 41 645007_1]
atha yat dvis aṅgulyā prāśnāti sa yat prathamam prāśnāti tena prāṇa apānau tṛpyataḥ | [JB, 1, 41 645008_1]
tam prāṇa apānau āhatuḥ śraddhā te mā vigāt sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ tṛpya svargam lokam āpnuhi iti | [JB, 1, 41 645009_1]
atha yat dvitīyam prāśnāti tena udāna apānau tṛpyataḥ | [JB, 1, 41 645010_1]
tam udāna apānau āhatuḥ śraddhā te mā vigāt sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ tṛpya svargam lokam āpnuhi iti | [JB, 1, 41 645011_1]
atha yat srucā prāśnāti tena samāna vyānau ca garbhān ca prīṇāti | [JB, 1, 41 645012_1]
tam samāna vyānau garbhāḥ ca āhuḥ śraddhā te mā vigāt sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ tṛpya svargam lokam āpnuhi iti | [JB, 1, 41 645013_1]
atha yat srucam niraśnāti tena deva janān prīṇāti | [JB, 1, 41 645014_1]
tam deva janāḥ āhuḥ śraddhā te mā vigāt sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ tṛpya svargam lokam āpnuhi iti | [JB, 1, 41 645015_1]
atha yat srucaḥ saṃkṣālanam ninayati tena vayāṃsi prīṇāti | [JB, 1, 41 645016_1]
tam vayāṃsi āhuḥ śraddhā te mā vigāt sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ tṛpya svargam lokam āpnuhi iti | [JB, 1, 41 645017_1]
atha yāḥ etāḥ srucaḥ nirṇijya udīcīḥ apaḥ utsiñcati tena ṛṣīn prīṇāti | [JB, 1, 41 645018_1]
tam ṛṣayaḥ āhuḥ śraddhā te mā vigāt sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ tṛpya svargam lokam āpnuhi iti | [JB, 1, 41 645019_1]
atha yat sthālī saṃkṣālanam ninayati tena sarpa janān prīṇāti | [JB, 1, 41 645020_1]
tam sarpa janāḥ āhuḥ śraddhā te mā vigāt sarvaiḥ kāmaiḥ tṛpya svargam lokam āpnuhi iti | [JB, 1, 41 645021_1]
atha yat paścāt vā purastāt vā parikramya dakṣiṇatas agnīnām āste prajāpatiḥ eva tat bhūtvā āste kam aham asmi kam mama iti | [JB, 1, 41 645022_1]
{JB, 1, 42}
bhṛguḥ ha vāruṇiḥ anūcānaḥ āsa | [JB, 1, 42 645023_1]
sa ha ati eva pitaram mene ati devān ati anyān brāhmaṇān anūcānān | [JB, 1, 42 645024_1]
sa ha varuṇaḥ īkṣāṃcakre na vai me putraḥ kiṃcana prajānāti hanta enam prajñāpayāni iti | [JB, 1, 42 645025_1]
tasya ha prāṇān abhijagrāha | [JB, 1, 42 645026_1]
sa ha tatāma | [JB, 1, 42 645027_1]
sa ha tāntaḥ param lokam jagāma | [JB, 1, 42 645028_1]
sa ha amuṣmin loke ājagāma | [JB, 1, 42 645029_1]
puruṣaḥ eva puruṣam saṃvṛścya atha enam jaghāsa | [JB, 1, 42 645030_1]
sa ha uvāca abhūt bata idam kim svid idam iti | [JB, 1, 42 645031_1]
tam ha ūcuḥ pitaram varuṇam pṛcchāsi sa te idam pravaktā iti | [JB, 1, 42 645032_1]
dvitīyam ha ājagāma | [JB, 1, 42 645033_1]
puruṣaḥ eva puruṣam ākrandayantam jaghāsa | [JB, 1, 42 645034_1]
sa ha uvāca abhūt bata idam kim svid idam iti | [JB, 1, 42 645035_1]

{JB, 1, 49}

{JB, 1, 50}

{JB, 1, 51}

trayo ha tvai grāmyāḥ paśavo 'juṣṭā durvarāha eḍakaḥ śvā | [JB, 1, 51 13]

tad u haike chādimuṣṭim eva nivapanto yanti gārhapatyād ā āhavanīyād idaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama ity etayarcā | [JB, 1, 52 1]
tad u tathā na kuryāt | [JB, 1, 52 2]
yo ha tatra brūyād āsān nvā ayaṃ yajamānasyāvāpsīt kṣipre parān āsān āvapsyate jyeṣṭhagṛhyaṃ rotsyatīti tathā haiva syāt | [JB, 1, 52 3]
ittham eva kuryāt | [JB, 1, 52 4]
udapātraṃ vaivodakamaṇḍaluṃ vādāya gārhapatyād ā āhavanīyān ninayann iyād idaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama ity etayaivarcā | [JB, 1, 52 5]
devapavitraṃ vā etad yad ṛk | [JB, 1, 52 6]
devapavitram etad yad āpaḥ | [JB, 1, 52 7]
tad yad evātra yajñasyāśāntaṃ bhavati yad amedhyam āpo vai tasya sarvasya śāntiḥ | [JB, 1, 52 8]
adbhir evainat tacchamayanti | [JB, 1, 52 9]
{JB, 1, 53}
tad āhur yad etasya dīrghasattriṇo 'gnihotraṃ juhvato 'gnihotraṃ duhyamānaṃ skandet kiṃ tatra karma kā prāyaścittir iti | [JB, 1, 53 1]
yad eva tatra sthālyāṃ pariśiṣṭaṃ syāt tena juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 53 2]
yady u nīcī sthālī syād api vā bhidyeta kiṃ tatra karma kā prāyaścittir iti | [JB, 1, 53 3]
skannaprāyaścittyaivābhimṛśya askann adhita ity atha yad anyad vindet tena juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 53 4]
yadā vai skandaty atha dhīyate | [JB, 1, 53 5]
reto vai payo yonir iyam | [JB, 1, 53 6]
yonyām evaitad retaḥ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [JB, 1, 53 7]
anuṣṭhyāsya retaḥ siktaṃ prajāyate ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 53 8]
amuto vai parjanyaḥ skandatīhauṣadhayo vanaspatayo jāyante | [JB, 1, 53 9]
puruṣād retaḥ skandati paśubhyaḥ | [JB, 1, 53 10]
tata idaṃ sarvaṃ prajātam | [JB, 1, 53 11]
sa vidyād upa mā devāḥ prābhūvan prajātir me bhūyasy abhūc chreyān bhaviṣyāmīti tathā haiva syāt | [JB, 1, 53 12]
atho yatraitat skannaṃ tad udapātraṃ vaivodakamaṇḍaluṃ vopaninayed bhūr bhuvaḥ svar ity etābhir vyāhṛtibhiḥ | [JB, 1, 53 13]
etā vai vyāhṛtayaḥ sarvaprāyaścittayaḥ | [JB, 1, 53 14]
tad anena sarveṇa prāyaścittiṃ kurute | [JB, 1, 53 15]
{JB, 1, 54}
athaitāni kapālāni saṃcitya yatrāhavanīyasya bhasmoddhṛtaṃ syāt tad upanikiret | [JB, 1, 54 1]
etad evātra karma | [JB, 1, 54 2]
atho khalv āhur yat prāca uddrutasya skandet kiṃ tatra karma kā prāyaścittir iti | [JB, 1, 54 3]
yad eva tatra sruci pariśiṣṭaṃ syāt tena juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 54 4]

tad u haike tata eva pratyetyonnayanti | [JB, 1, 54 7]
tad u tathā na kuryāt | [JB, 1, 54 8]
yo ha tatra brūyād yad anenāgnihotreṇācikīrṣīn nyavṛtat tasmān nāsyedaṃ svargyam iva bhaviṣyatīti tathā haiva syāt | [JB, 1, 54 9]
ittham eva kuryāt | [JB, 1, 54 10]
yatraiva skandet tad upaviśet | [JB, 1, 54 11]
athāsmin sthālīm āhareyuḥ sruvaṃ ca srucaṃ ca nirṇijya | [JB, 1, 54 12]
tad ada evāsyonneṣyāmīty uktaṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 54 13]
atha yathonnītam unnīya samidham ādāya prāk preyāt | [JB, 1, 54 14]
tad yathā pratyutthāyāmitrān paced evam evaitad avṛttiṃ pāpmānam apahatyāhutiṃ prāpnoti | [JB, 1, 54 15]
tad u haika upeva labhante 'hutaṃ tasya yasyāgnihotrocchiṣṭena juhvati yātayāmaṃ hy etad iti vadantaḥ | [JB, 1, 54 16]
tad u tathā na vidyāt | [JB, 1, 54 17]
yadā vā etad ayātayāmaṃ bhavaty athaitasyāpi havirātañcanaṃ kurvanti | [JB, 1, 54 18]
{JB, 1, 55}

{JB, 1, 62}

{JB, 1, 64}

atha u ha enayā pāpmanā vyāvṛtsyamānaḥ yajeta | [JB, 1, 64 645426_1]

{JB, 1, 65}

{JB, 1, 67}

{JB, 1, 73}

{JB, 1, 74}
namaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ pūrvasadbhyoṃ namaḥ sākaṃniṣadbhyom | [JB, 1, 74 1]
yuñje vācaṃ śatapadīṃ gāye sahasravartanīm | [JB, 1, 74 2.1]
gāyatraṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ jagad viśvā rūpāṇi saṃbhṛtam | [JB, 1, 74 2.2]
devā okāṃsi cakrira iti | [JB, 1, 74 2.3]
yan namaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ pūrvasadbhya iti pitaro vā atra pūrva upasīdanti | [JB, 1, 74 3]
sa tebhya evaitan namaskaroti | [JB, 1, 74 4]
namaḥ sākaṃniṣadbhya iti yair eva brāhmaṇaiḥ sahopasīdaty ārtvijyaṃ kariṣyaṃs tebhya evaitan namaskaroti | [JB, 1, 74 5]
yuñje vācaṃ śatapadīm iti vācam evaitac chatapadīṃ yuṅkte | [JB, 1, 74 6]
gāye sahasravartanīm iti yuktām evainām etat sahasravartanīṃ bhūtāṃ gāyati | [JB, 1, 74 7]
gāyatraṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ jagad ity etāni vai trīṇi savanāni tāny evaitāny ātman parigṛhṇīte | [JB, 1, 74 8]
viśvā rūpāṇi saṃbhṛtam iti yajño vai viśvā rūpāṇi yajñam evaitena saṃbharati | [JB, 1, 74 9]

{JB, 1, 75}
kusurbindo hauddālakiḥ somānām ujjagau | [JB, 1, 75 1]
tam u hāsitamṛgā iti kaśyapānāṃ putrā ūcuḥ ko nu no 'yaṃ nṛśaṃsako 'nta udgāyaty eta imam anuvyāhariṣyāma iti | [JB, 1, 75 2]
te 'nuvyāhariṣyanta āstāvam upaseduḥ | [JB, 1, 75 3]
sa hovāca namo brāhmaṇā astu purā vā aham adya prātaranuvākād gāyatreṇa viśvarūpāsu yajñaṃ samasthāpayaṃ sa yathā gobhir gavāyam itvā śramaṇam abalam anusaṃnuded evaṃ vāvedaṃ yajñaśarīram anusaṃnudāma iti | [JB, 1, 75 4]

{JB, 1, 76}

{JB, 1, 77}

{JB, 1, 78}

te 'śrāmyan | [JB, 1, 78 5]

{JB, 1, 79}
saṃmukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvābhimṛśati śyenā ajirā ṛtasya garbhāḥ prayuto napātaḥ parvatānāṃ kakubha ā nas taṃ vīraṃ vahata yaṃ bahava upajīvāmo 'bhiśastikṛtam anabhiśastenyam anyasyābhiśastyāḥ kartāram iti | [JB, 1, 79 1]
ā haivāsya vīro jāyate 'bhiśastikṛd anabhiśastenyo 'nyasyābhiśastyāḥ kartā | [JB, 1, 79 2]
droṇakalaśam adhyūhatīdam ahaṃ māṃ brahmavarcase 'dhyūhāmīti | [JB, 1, 79 3]
yady asyāvaruddho rājanyaḥ syād vimukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvā tūṣṇīṃ droṇakalaśam adhyūhya tam avahvārayan dakṣiṇā nirūhed idam aham amuṃ viśo nirūhāmīdam asya rāṣṭraṃ nyubjāmīti nyañcaṃ droṇakalaśaṃ nyubjet | [JB, 1, 79 4]
sammukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvā yo 'sya rājanyaḥ syāt tasya nāma gṛhītvā droṇakalaśam adhyūhed idam aham amuṃ viśy adhyūhāmīti | [JB, 1, 79 5]
apetaro rudhyate 'vetaro gacchati | [JB, 1, 79 6]
sa yady enam avagatya nādriyeta taṃ kāmayetātraivāntaravaruddho 'stv iti | [JB, 1, 79 7]
vimukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvā tūṣṇīṃ droṇakalaśam adhyūhyopāṃśusavana iti grāvā tam upariṣṭād abhinidadhyād idam aham amuṣmin viśam adhyūhāmīti | [JB, 1, 79 8]
abhiprakṣīṇānāhīnaṃ viṭ tiṣṭhati | [JB, 1, 79 9]
sa yady enaṃ viditvopadhāved asmin vāvedaṃ brāhmaṇe 'dhy āsa yad idam asyeva ca neva ceti sammukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvā droṇakalaśam adhyūhed idam aham amuṃ viśy adhyūhāmīti | [JB, 1, 79 10]
īśe svānām apainaṃ svāś cāyanty anantaravaruddho bhavati | [JB, 1, 79 11]
{JB, 1, 80}

{JB, 1, 81}
sa yat prathamam apāhan sā kṛṣṇāvirabhavat | [JB, 1, 81 1]
yad dvitīyam apāhan sā dhūmrāvirabhavat | [JB, 1, 81 2]
yat tṛtīyam apāhan sā phalguny avirabhavat | [JB, 1, 81 3]
sa yaṃ kāmayeta pāpīyān syād iti kṛṣṇam asya pavitre 'pyasyet pāpīyān eva bhavati | [JB, 1, 81 4]

atha yaṃ kāmayeta śreyān syād rucam aśnuvīteti phalgunam asya pavitraṃ kuryācchreyān eva bhavati rucam aśnute | [JB, 1, 81 6]
asti hi tatrāpy ādityasya nyaktaṃ | [JB, 1, 81 7]
tad antareṣe avahṛtya saṃmārṣṭi vasavas tvā saṃmṛjantu gāyatreṇa chandasā rudrās tvā saṃmṛjantu traiṣṭubhena chandasādityās tvā saṃmṛjantu jāgatena chandaseti | [JB, 1, 81 8]

{JB, 1, 82}

kā tasya prāyaścittir ity āhuḥ | [JB, 1, 82 2]
apa upaspṛśeyuḥ | [JB, 1, 82 3]
āpo vai sarvasya śāntiḥ | [JB, 1, 82 4]
adbhir evainaṃ tac chamayanti | [JB, 1, 82 5]

tayāparigṛhītayā yajñaṃ tanute | [JB, 1, 82 11]

vāg vai vekurā | [JB, 1, 82 14]
brahma vāk | [JB, 1, 82 15]

{JB, 1, 83}
araṇyam iva vā ete yanti ye bahiṣpavamānaṃ sarpanti | [JB, 1, 83 1]
tān īśvaro rakṣo vā hantor anyā vā naṃṣṭrā | [JB, 1, 83 2]
atha dvitīyāṃ juhoti sūryo mā devo divyebhyo rakṣobhyaḥ pātu vāta āntarikṣebhyo 'gniḥ pārthivebhyaḥ svāheti | [JB, 1, 83 3]

tam etad atrāptvāstuvan | [JB, 1, 83 7]

yajño vāva daivyo vājī | [JB, 1, 83 10]

atha kiṃ yo daivyaṃ vājinam aśāntam asaṃmṛṣṭam ārohāt | [JB, 1, 83 12]
{JB, 1, 84}
adhvaryuḥ prastaraṃ haran sarpati | [JB, 1, 84 1]
tam anumantrayata etad ahaṃ daivyaṃ vājinaṃ saṃmārjmīti | [JB, 1, 84 2]
saṃmṛṣṭam evainaṃ śāntam ārohati nārtim ārcchati | [JB, 1, 84 3]

ya in nu mānuṣāya kṣetrapataye 'procyāvasyati tam in nu sa hinasti vā pra vā yāpayati | [JB, 1, 84 5]
atha kiṃ yo daivyāya kṣetrapataye 'procyāvasyāt | [JB, 1, 84 6]
somodgāyodgāya somety āha | [JB, 1, 84 7]

mahyaṃ tejase mahyaṃ brahmavarcasāya mahyam annādyāya mahyaṃ bhūmne mahyaṃ puṣṭyai mahyaṃ prajananāya prajānāṃ bhūmne prajānāṃ puṣṭyai prajānāṃ prajananāya somasya rājño rājyāya mama grāmaṇeyāyeti | [JB, 1, 84 10]

te ha smāsmai kāmāḥ samṛdhyante | [JB, 1, 84 13]

tayābhyaveyāt | [JB, 1, 84 17]
tayodeyāt | [JB, 1, 84 18]

{JB, 1, 85}
prāṇān vāvaitat saṃtatya svargaṃ lokaṃ sarpanti yad antar havirdhāne grahān gṛhītvā bahiṣpavamānaṃ sarpanti | [JB, 1, 85 1]

svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyā anapavyāthāya | [JB, 1, 85 8]

pāṅkto yajñaḥ | [JB, 1, 85 18]

{JB, 1, 86}

yasyāṃ varṣīyasyām ṛci hrasīyo hrasīyasyāṃ vā varṣīyas tām ānāyakāmaḥ pratipadaṃ kurvīta | [JB, 1, 96 12]
varṣīyasā vā eṣa hrasīyaḥ prepsatīti hrasīyasā vā varṣīyaḥ | [JB, 1, 96 13]
pra hrasīyasā varṣīya āpnoti ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 96 14]
eṣa devo amartya iti pratipadaṃ kurvīta yaḥ kāmayetāham evaikadhā śreṣṭhaḥ svānāṃ syāṃ rucam aśnuvīyeti | [JB, 1, 96 15]
eṣa eṣa ity evaināñ jyaiṣṭhyāya śraiṣṭhyāyābhivadati | [JB, 1, 96 16]
ekadhaiva śreṣṭhaḥ svānāṃ bhavati rucam aśnute | [JB, 1, 96 17]
īśvaro ha tv asyāparaḥ prajāyām etādṛṅ vīro 'nājanitoḥ | [JB, 1, 96 18]
eṣa eva nāto 'nya itīva hy enaṃ vāg abhivadati | [JB, 1, 96 19]
tad u tvai tan na tathā | [JB, 1, 96 20]
devo amartya iti vā āha | [JB, 1, 96 21]
adevaś ca ha vai sa martyaś ca yasya vīrasya sato vīro vīryavān nājāyate | [JB, 1, 96 22]
atha ha vai sa eva devaḥ so 'martyo yasya vīrasya sato vīro vīryavān ājāyate | [JB, 1, 96 23]
ā hāsya vīrasya sato vīro vīryavāñ jāyate saṃdhīyate prajayā na vyavacchidyate | [JB, 1, 96 24]
{JB, 1, 97}

{JB, 1, 103}

{JB, 1, 107}

{JB, 1, 108}

{JB, 1, 138}

{JB, 1, 140}
vicchinnam iva vā etat sāma pratihāraṃ prati | [JB, 1, 140 1]

{JB, 1, 141}

{JB, 1, 142}
devā vā asurān yudham upaprayanto 'bruvan yan no vāmaṃ vasu tad apanidhāya yudhyāmahai yad adya kasmiṃścid bhūte 'bhyavadhāvāmeti | [JB, 1, 142 1]
prāṇā vāva teṣāṃ vāmaṃ vasv āsīt | [JB, 1, 142 2]
tad apanidhāya yudham upaparāyan | [JB, 1, 142 3]
tad ekadhā bhūtvāsṛjamānam atiṣṭhad ṛcaḥ sāmāni yajūṃṣi gām aśvam ajām aviṃ vrīhiṃ yavaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ rājanyaṃ vaiśyaṃ śūdraṃ yad idaṃ kiṃcit tat sarvam | [JB, 1, 142 4]
tad ebhya ācakṣatedaṃ vai vas tad vāmaṃ vasv ekadhā bhūtvāsṛjamānaṃ tiṣṭhatīti | [JB, 1, 142 5]
te devā asurān ajayan | [JB, 1, 142 6]
te vijigyānāḥ punar āyanta ekaṃ bhūtam abhyavāyan | [JB, 1, 142 7]
tan na vyajānatedaṃ mama vāmam idaṃ mameti | [JB, 1, 142 8]
te 'bruvan vīdaṃ bhajāmahā iti | [JB, 1, 142 9]
tasya vibhāge na samapādayan | [JB, 1, 142 10]
tad evainān abravīt sarvān eva vo mayā stoṣyanti sarvān vo 'ham avaiṣyāmi mā mā vibhagdhvam iti | [JB, 1, 142 11]
tad yad gāyatrīṣu stuvanti tenāgneyam | [JB, 1, 142 12]
gāyatro hy agniḥ | [JB, 1, 142 13]
yat pṛṣṭhaṃ mādhyaṃdinaṃ tenaindram | [JB, 1, 142 14]
yat kavatīṣu stuvanti tena prājāpatyam | [JB, 1, 142 15]
yad aniruktaṃ tena vaiśvadevam | [JB, 1, 142 16]
yan maitrāvaruṇāya stuvanti tena maitrāvaruṇam | [JB, 1, 142 17]
tad enān abravīt sṛjadhvaṃ mad iti | [JB, 1, 142 18]
tatheti | [JB, 1, 142 19]
tad abhyasvaran | [JB, 1, 142 20]
tad abruvan sṛjasveti | [JB, 1, 142 21]
{JB, 1, 143}

{JB, 1, 154}

{JB, 1, 155}
nety abruvan sādhuvibhaktā no lokās tān na śakṣyāmaḥ saṃlobhayitum iti | [JB, 1, 155 1]

tenāstuvata | [JB, 1, 155 18]

{JB, 1, 156}

{JB, 1, 161}

{JB, 1, 179}

{JB, 1, 201}

{JB, 1, 226}

{JB, 1, 227}

{JB, 1, 231}

{JB, 1, 232}

{JB, 1, 233}

{JB, 1, 234}
puraś cakraṃ patho bile taṃ cakram abhivartate yo 'sampannena yajate 'pāko yajñena devair yad dadāti tad evāsya na lokam abhigacchatīti | [JB, 1, 234 1]

{JB, 1, 235}
etaddha vai paramaṃ vācaḥ krāntaṃ yad daśeti | [JB, 1, 235 1]

dve stotriye upaprastutye | [JB, 1, 235 15]

{JB, 1, 236}

gacchati paramatāṃ ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 248 14]
atha ha smāhāruṇiḥ kiṃ so 'bhicaret kiṃ vābhicāryamāṇa ādriyeta ya etaṃ trivṛtaṃ vajraṃ tribhṛṣṭim acchidram acchambaṭkāriṇam ahar ahar imān lokān anuvartamānaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 248 15]

{JB, 1, 249}

{JB, 1, 250}

{JB, 1, 252}

{JB, 1, 253}

ya evainam upavadati sa ārtim ārcchati | [JB, 1, 256 3]
sa ya enam upavadet taṃ brūyāt pūrṇam evāham etaṃ sāṅgaṃ satanuṃ sarvaṃ yajñaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 256 4]
sa yat tvam atronaṃ vettha tat tvayaivāpidadhānīti | [JB, 1, 256 5]
sa evārtim ārcchati ya evaṃ vidvāṃsam upavadati | [JB, 1, 256 6]
sa eṣa prajāpatir agniṣṭomo 'mūm ekaviṃśī3ṃ yajñāyajñīyasyāsu bahiṣpavamānīṣu navasu pratyupadhāya śaya etā dviṣṭanā virājo duhānaḥ pañca pañcadaśāni pañca saptadaśāni | [JB, 1, 256 7]
tā eva pañca dvātriṃśinīr virājaḥ | [JB, 1, 256 8]
duhe ha vai virājaṃ sarvān kāmān ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 256 9]
na haivaṃvido 'nṛtaṃ cana vadato yajñaḥ sravati | [JB, 1, 256 10]
sravati ha vā anṛtaṃ vadato yajño 'tho ha pūyati | [JB, 1, 256 11]
no ha tvāvaivaṃvido yajñaḥ sravati na pūyati | [JB, 1, 256 12]
tasmāt kurupañcālā dviṣṭanāṃ na duhre | [JB, 1, 256 13]
prajāpater ha sā | [JB, 1, 256 14]
tasmād v anya udantā duhre | [JB, 1, 256 15]
na hi te tāṃ viduḥ | [JB, 1, 256 16]
tasmād v anya udantā aśanāyukatarā iva | [JB, 1, 256 17]
{JB, 1, 257}
sa eṣa prajāpatir agniṣṭomaḥ parimaṇḍalo bhūtvānanto bhūtvā śaye | [JB, 1, 257 1]
tadanukṛtīdam apy anyā devatāḥ parimaṇḍalāḥ parimaṇḍala ādityaḥ parimaṇḍalaś candramāḥ parimaṇḍalā dyauḥ parimaṇḍalam antarikṣaṃ parimaṇḍaleyaṃ pṛthivī | [JB, 1, 257 2]
api yad idaṃ puruṣe divyaṃ tat parimaṇḍalam | [JB, 1, 257 3]

imāny eva catvāry ūrvaṣṭhīvāny ājyāni | [JB, 1, 257 7]
yad avācīnaṃ nābheḥ sa tricchandā mādhyaṃdinaḥ | [JB, 1, 257 8]
pṛṣṭhāny eva pṛṣṭhāni | [JB, 1, 257 9]
ayam ārbhavaḥ | [JB, 1, 257 10]

sa hovācordhva eva puruṣam anvāyatta iti | [JB, 1, 257 13]
evaṃ ha tad uvāca | [JB, 1, 257 14]

ya u enaṃ pratyañcaṃ veda pratyaṅ bhūtiṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 257 16]

imāny ājyāni | [JB, 1, 257 18]

pratyaṅ bhūtiṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 257 23]

{JB, 1, 258}
tasyaiṣa ślokaḥ | [JB, 1, 258 1]
yad asya pūrvam aparaṃ tad asya yad v asyāparaṃ tad v asya pūrvam aher iva sarpaṇaṃ śākalasya na vijānāmi yatarat purastād iti | [JB, 1, 258 2]
śakalo ha gaupāyano yajñaṃ mimāna iyāya | [JB, 1, 258 3]
sa ha smaitan na vijānāti katarad yajñasya pūrvaṃ katarad aparaṃ katarad aṇīyaḥ katarat sthavīya iti | [JB, 1, 258 4]
tad āhuḥ kuto yajñasyāṇiṣṭham iti | [JB, 1, 258 5]
yato variṣṭham iti | [JB, 1, 258 6]
kuto variṣṭham iti | [JB, 1, 258 7]
yato 'ṇiṣṭham iti | [JB, 1, 258 8]
bahiṣpavamānaṃ vāva prati yajño 'ṇiṣṭhaḥ | [JB, 1, 258 9]
tad idaṃ pādāv avocat | [JB, 1, 258 10]
pādau vai prati puruṣo 'ṇiṣṭhaḥ | [JB, 1, 258 11]
tad v eva variṣṭhaḥ | [JB, 1, 258 12]
padbhyāṃ hy eti | [JB, 1, 258 13]
kuto variṣṭha iti | [JB, 1, 258 14]
yato 'ṇiṣṭha iti | [JB, 1, 258 15]
yajñāyajñīyaṃ vāva prati yajño 'ṇiṣṭhaḥ | [JB, 1, 258 16]
tad idaṃ śiro 'vocat | [JB, 1, 258 17]
śiro vai prati puruṣo 'ṇiṣṭhaḥ | [JB, 1, 258 18]
tad v eva variṣṭhaḥ | [JB, 1, 258 19]
akṣibhyāṃ hi paśyann eti | [JB, 1, 258 20]
tad āhur yad ūrdhvo yajñas tāyeta devā eva jīveyur na manuṣyāḥ | [JB, 1, 258 21]
yad arvāṅ tāyeta manuṣyā eva jīveyur na devā iti | [JB, 1, 258 22]
ūrdhvaś ca ha vai yajñas tāyate 'rvāṅ ca | [JB, 1, 258 23]
atho ha tiryaṅ | [JB, 1, 258 24]
tad yat pṛccheyuḥ kadriyaṅ yajña iti | [JB, 1, 258 25]
ūrdhva iti brūyāt | [JB, 1, 258 26]
atho arvāṅ iti | [JB, 1, 258 27]
atho tiryaṅṅ iti | [JB, 1, 258 28]
sarvā eva diśa iti brūyāt | [JB, 1, 258 29]
sarvā u ha vai diśa evaṃvido yajñas tato bhavati | [JB, 1, 258 30]
kurupañcālā ha brahmodyam ūdire | [JB, 1, 258 31]
te ha śvānaṃ saṃveṣṭitaṃ śayānam upeyuḥ | [JB, 1, 258 32]
te hocur asminn u eva no vijayo 'dhy astv iti | [JB, 1, 258 33]
te ha pañcālāḥ kurūn papracchuḥ kim asya yajñasyeveti | [JB, 1, 258 34]
taddha na pratyūcuḥ | [JB, 1, 258 35]
sa hovāca vāsiṣṭhaś caikitāneyo yathā vā asāv ado 'mūm ekaviṃśī3ṃ yajñāyajñīyasyāsu bahiṣpavamānīṣu navasu pratyupadhāya śaya evaṃ vā ayam idam ubhāv antau saṃdhāya śaye | [JB, 1, 258 36]
tasya vā ayaṃ yajñakrator anayā śayyayā rūpaṃ nigacchati | [JB, 1, 258 37]
tasmād imam anukthyaṃ santaṃ vibhūtīti | [JB, 1, 258 38]
tena ha jigyuḥ | [JB, 1, 258 39]
{JB, 1, 259}
dvir ha vai yajamāno jāyate mithunād anyaj jāyate yajñād anyat | [JB, 1, 259 1]
tad yan mithunāj jāyate tad asmai lokāya jāyate | [JB, 1, 259 2]
atha yad yajñāj jāyate tad amuṣmai lokāya jāyate gandharvalokāya jāyate devalokāya jāyate svargāya lokāya jāyate | [JB, 1, 259 3]
yajño vai yajamānaḥ | [JB, 1, 259 4]
yajñaḥ somo rājā | [JB, 1, 259 5]

sa rūpāṇāṃ vikartā | [JB, 1, 259 10]

{JB, 1, 260}
gāyatrīṃ gāyati | [JB, 1, 260 1]

{JB, 1, 261}
tāṃ balavad upabdimatīṃ nighātaṃ gāyet | [JB, 1, 261 1]

{JB, 1, 262}
sabheyaḥ | [JB, 1, 262 1]
evaṃ hy etat kurupañcālā aviduḥ | [JB, 1, 262 2]
tasmāt kurupañcāleṣu sarvair vīraiḥ saha vīra ājāyate | [JB, 1, 262 3]
atha yarhy etad udantāḥ purā nāvediṣus tasmād udanteṣu purā sarvair vīraiḥ saha vīro nājani | [JB, 1, 262 4]
atha yata idam udantān evaṃvidaś ca sacanta evaṃvidaś cainān yājayanti tato hārvācīnam udanteṣu sarvair vīraiḥ saha vīra ājāyate | [JB, 1, 262 5]
kurupañcālā ha brahmodyam ūdire | [JB, 1, 262 6]
te ha pañcālāḥ kurūn papracchuḥ kiṃ vayaṃ tad yajñe 'kurma yenāsmāsu sarvair vīraiḥ saha vīra ājāyata iti | [JB, 1, 262 7]
taddha na pratyūcuḥ | [JB, 1, 262 8]
tena haināñ jigyuḥ | [JB, 1, 262 9]
te yat pratyavakṣyan yasmād vayam evaṃvidaś ca sma evaṃvidaś ca no yājayanti tenāsmāsu sarvair vīraiḥ saha vīra ājāyata iti | [JB, 1, 262 10]
sarvair ha vā asmād vīraiḥ saha vīra ājāyate ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 262 11]
tad āhur vigeyā dhurā3 'vigeyā3 iti | [JB, 1, 262 12]
vigeyā ity āhuḥ | [JB, 1, 262 13]
{JB, 1, 263}
kuravaḥ | [JB, 1, 263 1]
gāyatraṃ vai prātassavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanam | [JB, 1, 263 2]
tad evānuṣṭub anvāyattā | [JB, 1, 263 3]
sa yad gāyatre sati prātassavane gāyatrīṃ gāyati brahma vai gāyatrī brahma prātassavanaṃ sva eva tad āyatane brahma dadhāti | [JB, 1, 263 4]
atha yat triṣṭubhaṃ gāyati kṣatraṃ vai triṣṭub etāni vai kṣatre śilpāni hastī niṣko 'śvatarīratho 'śvaratho rukmaḥ kaṃsas tāny eva tad āhṛtya brahmaṇy anakti | [JB, 1, 263 5]
atha yaj jagatīṃ gāyati viḍ vai jagaty etāni vai viśi śilpāni goaśvaṃ hastihiraṇyam ajāvikaṃ vrīhiyavās tilamāṣāḥ sarpiḥ kṣīraṃ rayiḥ puṣṭis tāny eva tad āhṛtya brahmaṇy anakti | [JB, 1, 263 6]
tad evānuṣṭub anvāyattā | [JB, 1, 263 7]
atha yad anuṣṭubhaṃ gāyaty ānuṣṭubho vai śūdraś śūdrād eva tad āhṛtya brahmaṇy anakti | [JB, 1, 263 8]
{JB, 1, 264}
tad yathā tūṇiṃ kaśanair vihanyād evam evaitāni sarvāṇi śilpāny āhṛtya brahmaṇy anakti | [JB, 1, 264 1]
tasmād vigeyā iti | [JB, 1, 264 2]
yato ha vā idam etā vigīyante tato hedaṃ brāhmaṇā jīyante | [JB, 1, 264 3]
atha yarhi etā na vijagur annāḍhyā ha brāhmaṇā āsuḥ | [JB, 1, 264 4]
ekāpacchādevāhasmāsata ekaśakaṭevāvaśehasmadamayitvā satyayajñaḥ pauluṣir yāti | [JB, 1, 264 5]
atha yata idam etā vigīyante tato haitāni śilpāni brāhmaṇeṣv adhigamyante | [JB, 1, 264 6]
gāyatrīṃ purastād gāyati gāyatrīm upariṣṭāt | [JB, 1, 264 7]
brahma vai gāyatrī | [JB, 1, 264 8]
brahmaṇaiva tad etāny ubhayataś śilpāni parigṛhṇāti | [JB, 1, 264 9]
brahmaṇā hainam etāny ubhayataś śilpāni parigṛhītāny upatiṣṭhante ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 264 10]
na vigeyā ity āhuḥ pañcālāḥ | [JB, 1, 264 11]
svayaṃvigītā vā etā yaddhuraḥ | [JB, 1, 264 12]
anusavanaṃ vā etā vigāyann abhyārohati | [JB, 1, 264 13]
atha yad enān pāpī kīrtir anūttiṣṭhati vyagāsiṣur iti yau vai yudhyete yāv ṛtīyete tāv āhur vyagāsiṣṭām iti | [JB, 1, 264 14]
atho ye rāṣṭre vyavabhindāne tiṣṭhata iti | [JB, 1, 264 15]
{JB, 1, 265}
gāyatraṃ vai prātassavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanam | [JB, 1, 265 1]
tad evānuṣṭub anvāyattā | [JB, 1, 265 2]
sa yad gāyatre sati prātassavane gāyatrīṃ gāyati brahma vai gāyatrī brahmaiva tad brāhmaṇasya sve 'nvābhajati | [JB, 1, 265 3]
so 'syāditsata upajihīrṣate | [JB, 1, 265 4]
atho asyaiva tat | [JB, 1, 265 5]
sve 'nu hy enam ābhajati | [JB, 1, 265 6]
atha yat triṣṭubhaṃ gāyati kṣatraṃ vai triṣṭup kṣatriyam eva tad brāhmaṇasya sve 'nvābhajati | [JB, 1, 265 7]
so 'syāditsata upajihīrṣate | [JB, 1, 265 8]
atho asyaiva tat | [JB, 1, 265 9]
sve 'nu hy enam ābhajati | [JB, 1, 265 10]
atha yaj jagatīṃ gāyati viḍ vai jagatī vaiśyam eva tad brāhmaṇasya sve 'nvābhajati | [JB, 1, 265 11]
so 'syāditsata upajihīrṣate | [JB, 1, 265 12]
atho asyaiva tat | [JB, 1, 265 13]
sve 'nu hy enam ābhajati | [JB, 1, 265 14]
tad evānuṣṭub anvāyattā | [JB, 1, 265 15]
atha yad anuṣṭubhaṃ gāyaty ānuṣṭubho vai śūdraś śūdram eva tad brāhmaṇasya sve 'nvābhajati | [JB, 1, 265 16]
so 'syāditsata upajihīrṣate | [JB, 1, 265 17]
atho asyaiva tat | [JB, 1, 265 18]
sve 'nu hy enam ābhajati | [JB, 1, 265 19]
yady āvṛṅ nāthopavaṃke naiva lipsate | [JB, 1, 265 20]
tasmān na vigeyā iti | [JB, 1, 265 21]
yato ha vā idam etā vigīyante tato hedaṃ brāhmaṇā jīyante | [JB, 1, 265 22]
atha yarhy etā na vijagur ajyeyā ha brāhmaṇā āsuḥ | [JB, 1, 265 23]
{JB, 1, 266}
gāyatraṃ vai prātassavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanam | [JB, 1, 266 1]
tad evānuṣṭub anvāyattā | [JB, 1, 266 2]
sa yad gāyatraṃ sat prātassavanaṃ sarvam eva gāyatraṃ gāyati brahmaṇa eva taṃ kevalam uddhāram uddharati | [JB, 1, 266 3]
so 'sya brahmaṇaḥ kevala uddhāra uddhṛto bhavati | [JB, 1, 266 4]
atha yat traiṣṭubhaṃ san mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ gāyatreṇaivānupratipadyate brāhmaṇam eva tat kṣatriyasya sve 'nvābhajati | [JB, 1, 266 5]
so 'smai ditsati śraddhayā karmaṇopacāreṇa | [JB, 1, 266 6]
yadā vai kṣatriyaṃ śraddhā vindati brāhmaṇaṃ vāva sa tarhīcchati | [JB, 1, 266 7]
so 'smai dadāti | [JB, 1, 266 8]
atha yaj jāgataṃ sat tṛtīyasavanaṃ gāyatreṇaivānupratipadyate brāhmaṇam eva tad vaiśyasya sve 'nvābhajati | [JB, 1, 266 9]
so 'smai ditsati śraddhayā karmaṇopacāreṇa | [JB, 1, 266 10]
yadā vai vaiśyaṃ śraddhā vindati brāhmaṇaṃ vāva sa tarhīcchati | [JB, 1, 266 11]
so 'smai dadāti | [JB, 1, 266 12]
tad evānuṣṭub anvāyattā | [JB, 1, 266 13]
atha yad anuṣṭubhaṃ gāyaty ānuṣṭubho vai śūdro brāhmaṇam eva tac chūdrasya sve 'nvābhajati | [JB, 1, 266 14]
so 'smai ditsati śraddhayā karmaṇopacāreṇa | [JB, 1, 266 15]
yadā vai śūdraṃ śraddhā vindati brāhmaṇaṃ vāva sa tarhīcchati | [JB, 1, 266 16]
so 'smai dadāti | [JB, 1, 266 17]
kevalaṃ svaṃ kurute | [JB, 1, 266 18]
apitvī kṣatre bhavaty apitvī viśi | [JB, 1, 266 19]
yāty antassthāṃ nāntassthāyāṃ jīyate | [JB, 1, 266 20]
upa hainaṃ śataṃ pariskandās tiṣṭhante | [JB, 1, 266 21]
atho bhūyāṃso ya evaṃ vidvān dhuro na vigāyatīti | [JB, 1, 266 22]
sa yadi vigāyed ado vidvān vigāyet | [JB, 1, 266 23]
yady u na vigāyed idaṃ vidvān na vigāyet | [JB, 1, 266 24]
ārtiḥ sā yo 'nyatarad eva vedeti ha smāha śāṭyāyaniḥ | [JB, 1, 266 25]
{JB, 1, 267}
retasyāṃ gāyati | [JB, 1, 267 1]
retas tat siñcati | [JB, 1, 267 2]
tad retaḥ siktaṃ gāyatryodvardhayati varṣīyasā chandasā | [JB, 1, 267 3]
tat triṣṭubhodvardhayati varṣīyasā chandasā | [JB, 1, 267 4]
taj jagatyodvardhayati varṣīyasaiva chandasā | [JB, 1, 267 5]
tad yad varṣīyasā varṣīyasā chandasodvardhayati tasmād vardhamānasya bhūyo bhūyo vīryaṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 267 6]
anuṣṭubhā niṣṭhāṃ gacchati hrasīyasaiva chandasā | [JB, 1, 267 7]
tasmād uttaravayase pratitarām ivāvavardhate | [JB, 1, 267 8]
pañcamyā niṣṭhāṃ gacchati | [JB, 1, 267 9]
tasmāt pañcame māsi garbhā vikriyante | [JB, 1, 267 10]
anuṣṭubhā vācā niṣṭhāṃ gacchati | [JB, 1, 267 11]
tasmād u jīrṇasya vācaṃ śuśrūṣante | [JB, 1, 267 12]
śiro vā etad yajñasya yad bahiṣpavamānam | [JB, 1, 267 13]
tad vai tat | [JB, 1, 267 14]
retasyaivāpi sarva ātmā | [JB, 1, 267 15]
{JB, 1, 268}
sa yad bahiṣpavamāne gāyatrīṃ gāyati prāṇo vai gāyatro gāyatraṃ śira eva tadāyatano vai prāṇo yac chiras sva eva tad āyatane prāṇaṃ dadhāti | [JB, 1, 268 1]
triṣṭubhaṃ gāyati | [JB, 1, 268 2]
cakṣur vai triṣṭup | [JB, 1, 268 3]
tām eva tad āhṛtya śīrṣan niyunakti | [JB, 1, 268 4]
yan niyunakti tasmān niyuktam iva cakṣuḥ | [JB, 1, 268 5]
tām anyatrāyatanāṃ satīṃ niyunakti mādhyaṃdināyatanām | [JB, 1, 268 6]
tāṃ yad anyatrāyatanāṃ satīṃ niyunakti tasmād uta jīvata eva cakṣur apakrāmati | [JB, 1, 268 7]
jagatīṃ gāyati | [JB, 1, 268 8]
śrotraṃ vai jagatī | [JB, 1, 268 9]
tām eva tad āhṛtya śīrṣan niyunakti | [JB, 1, 268 10]
yan niyunakti tasmān niyuktam iva śrotram | [JB, 1, 268 11]
tām anyatrāyatanāṃ satīṃ niyunakti tṛtīyasavanāyatanām | [JB, 1, 268 12]
tāṃ yad anyatrāyatanāṃ satīṃ niyunakti tasmād uta jīvata eva śrotram apakrāmati | [JB, 1, 268 13]
anuṣṭubhaṃ gāyati | [JB, 1, 268 14]
vāg vā anuṣṭup | [JB, 1, 268 15]
tām eva tad āhṛtya śīrṣan niyunakti | [JB, 1, 268 16]
yan niyunakti tasmān niyukteva vāk | [JB, 1, 268 17]
tām anyatrāyatanāṃ satīṃ niyunakti tṛtīyasavanāyatanāṃ vā sarvāyatanāṃ vā | [JB, 1, 268 18]
tāṃ yad anyatrāyatanāṃ satīṃ niyunakti tasmād uta jīvata eva vāg apakrāmati | [JB, 1, 268 19]
apānye prāṇāḥ krāmanti na prāṇaḥ | [JB, 1, 268 20]
{JB, 1, 269}
tad āhuḥ kiṃ tad yajñe kriyate yasmāj jīvata evānye prāṇā apakrāmanti na prāṇa iti | [JB, 1, 269 1]
sa brūyād yasmāt sva āyatane gāyatrīṃ gāyati tasmād yāvaj jīvati tāvat prāṇo nāpakrāmatīti | [JB, 1, 269 2]
atha ha vai dhurāṃ vijñāś ca saṃjñāś ca | [JB, 1, 269 3]
mano vai retasyā | [JB, 1, 269 4]
prāṇo gāyatrī | [JB, 1, 269 5]
cakṣus triṣṭup | [JB, 1, 269 6]
śrotraṃ jagatī | [JB, 1, 269 7]
vāg anuṣṭup | [JB, 1, 269 8]
manasā suhārdasaṃ ca durhārdasaṃ ca vijānāti | [JB, 1, 269 9]
prāṇena surabhi cāsurabhi ca vijānāti | [JB, 1, 269 10]
cakṣuṣā darśanīyaṃ cādarśanīyaṃ ca vijānāti | [JB, 1, 269 11]
śrotreṇa śravaṇīyaṃ cāśravaṇīyaṃ ca vijānāti | [JB, 1, 269 12]
vācā svādu cāsvādu ca vijānāti | [JB, 1, 269 13]
etā iha vijñāḥ | [JB, 1, 269 14]
vi ha vai jñāyate śreyān bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 269 15]
tā u eva saṃjñāḥ | [JB, 1, 269 16]
mano vai retasyā | [JB, 1, 269 17]
prāṇo gāyatrī | [JB, 1, 269 18]
cakṣus triṣṭup | [JB, 1, 269 19]
śrotraṃ jagatī | [JB, 1, 269 20]
vāg anuṣṭup | [JB, 1, 269 21]
retasyāyāṃ prastutāyāṃ yasya kāmayeta | [JB, 1, 269 22]
{JB, 1, 270}
tasya manasā mano dhyāyet | [JB, 1, 270 1]
gāyatryāṃ prastutāyāṃ yasya kāmayeta tasya prāṇena prāṇaṃ dhyāyet | [JB, 1, 270 2]
triṣṭubhi prastutāyāṃ yasya kāmayeta tasya cakṣuṣā cakṣur dhyāyet | [JB, 1, 270 3]
jagatyāṃ prastutāyāṃ yasya kāmayeta tasya śrotreṇa śrotraṃ dhyāyet | [JB, 1, 270 4]
anuṣṭubhi prastutāyāṃ yasya kāmayeta tasya vācā vācaṃ dhyāyet | [JB, 1, 270 5]
etā u ha saṃjñāḥ | [JB, 1, 270 6]
saṃ ha vai tena jānīte yena kāmayate 'nena saṃjānīyeti ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 270 7]
athaitā devadhuraś ca manuṣyadhuraś ca saṃdadhāti | [JB, 1, 270 8]
mano vai manuṣyadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 9]
āpo devadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 10]
retasyāyāṃ prastutāyāṃ manasāpaḥ saṃdadhyāt | [JB, 1, 270 11]
tad antarā yajamānasya mano 'vayātayet | [JB, 1, 270 12]
prāṇo vai manuṣyadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 13]
vāyur devadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 14]
gāyatryāṃ prastutāyāṃ prāṇena vāyuṃ saṃdadhyāt | [JB, 1, 270 15]
tad antarā yajamānasya prāṇam avayātayet | [JB, 1, 270 16]
cakṣur vai manuṣyadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 17]
ādityo devadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 18]
triṣṭubhi prastutāyāṃ cakṣuṣādityaṃ saṃdadhyāt | [JB, 1, 270 19]
tad antarā yajamānasya cakṣur avayātayet | [JB, 1, 270 20]
śrotraṃ vai manuṣyadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 21]
diśo devadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 22]
jagatyāṃ prastutāyāṃ śrotreṇa diśaḥ saṃdadhyāt | [JB, 1, 270 23]
tad antarā yajamānasya śrotram avayātayet | [JB, 1, 270 24]
vāg vai manuṣyadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 25]
pṛthivī devadhūḥ | [JB, 1, 270 26]

tad antarā yajamānasya vācam avayātayet | [JB, 1, 270 28]
etad vai devadhuraś ca manuṣyadhuraś ca saṃdadhāti | [JB, 1, 270 29]
etad vai devadhuraś ca manuṣyadhuraś ca saṃdhāya taṃ mṛtyuṃ tarati yaḥ svargaloke | [JB, 1, 270 30]
na haivaṃvit punar mriyate | [JB, 1, 270 31]
devatāsv ātmānam upasaṃdadhāti | [JB, 1, 270 32]
{JB, 1, 271}
athaiteṣāṃ mahatāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ samuditam āruṇer jīvalasya kārīrāder aṣāḍhasya sāvayasasyendradyumnasya bhāllabeyasyeti | [JB, 1, 271 1]
jīvalaś ca ha kārīrādir indradyumnaś ca bhāllabeyas tau hāruṇer ācāryasya sabhāgāv ājagmatuḥ | [JB, 1, 271 2]
te hāṣāḍhasya gṛheṣu śiśyire | [JB, 1, 271 3]
sa hovācāṣāḍha ām āruṇe yat sahaiva brahmacaryam acarāva sahānvabravīvahy atha kenedaṃ tvam asmān atyanūciṣe | [JB, 1, 271 4]
yad idaṃ tvam iyatpriyaḥ kīrter iyatpriyaś cakṣuṣa iyatpriyaḥ saner asi kena tvam idaṃ prāpitheti | [JB, 1, 271 5]
sa hovāca dhūrṣv evāhaṃ tad upāsa iti | [JB, 1, 271 6]
kiṃ tvaṃ tad dhūrṣūpāssa iti | [JB, 1, 271 7]
priyam iti | [JB, 1, 271 8]
ya āsāṃ priyam upāste kiṃ sa bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 271 9]
priya eva sa kīrteḥ priyaś cakṣuṣaḥ priyaḥ saner bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 271 10]
evam eva tvam asīti hocuḥ | [JB, 1, 271 11]
atha hocur jīvalaṃ kārīrādiṃ yad idaṃ tvam eva tasyārdhasya śreṣṭho 'si yasminn asy api tvā rājāno 'dhastād upāsate kena tvam idaṃ prāpitheti | [JB, 1, 271 12]
sa hovāca dhūrṣv evāhaṃ tad upāsa iti | [JB, 1, 271 13]
kiṃ tvaṃ tad dhūrṣūpāssa iti | [JB, 1, 271 14]
śriyam iti | [JB, 1, 271 15]
ya āsāṃ śriyam upāste kiṃ sa bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 271 16]
yasminn evārdhe bhavati tasya śreṣṭho bhavaty apy enaṃ rājāno 'dhastād upāsata iti | [JB, 1, 271 17]
evam eva tvam asīti hocuḥ | [JB, 1, 271 18]
atha hocur aṣāḍhaṃ sāvayasaṃ yad idaṃ tvaṃ śārkarākṣāṇāṃ vāva grāmaṇy evāsi kena tvam idaṃ prāpitheti | [JB, 1, 271 19]
sa hovāca dhūrṣv evāhaṃ tad upāsa iti | [JB, 1, 271 20]
kiṃ tvaṃ tad dhūrṣūpāssa iti | [JB, 1, 271 21]
jātam iti | [JB, 1, 271 22]
ya āsāṃ jātam upāste kiṃ sa bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 271 23]
yatraiva sajāto bhavati tad grāmaṇīr bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 271 24]
evam eva tvam asīti hocuḥ | [JB, 1, 271 25]
atha hocur indradyumnaṃ bhāllabeyaṃ yad idaṃ tavoparyupary anyān kīrtiś carati vivacanam evāsi kena tvam idaṃ prāpitheti | [JB, 1, 271 26]
sa hovāca dhūrṣv evāhaṃ tad upāsa iti | [JB, 1, 271 27]
kiṃ tvaṃ tad dhūrṣūpāssa iti | [JB, 1, 271 28]
yaśa iti | [JB, 1, 271 29]
ya āsāṃ yaśa upāste kiṃ sa bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 271 30]
uparyupary evāsyānyān kīrtiś carati vivacanam eva bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 271 31]
evam eva tvam asīti hocuḥ | [JB, 1, 271 32]
te hocur itthaṃ ced idam abhūt | [JB, 1, 271 33]
eta idaṃ saṃprabravāmahā iti | [JB, 1, 271 34]
{JB, 1, 272}
te hāruṇim ūcus tvaṃ vai na ācāryo 'si | [JB, 1, 272 1]
tvaṃ prathamo brūṣveti | [JB, 1, 272 2]
sa hovāca gāyatrīm evāhaṃ priyam upāsa iti | [JB, 1, 272 3]
prāṇo vai gāyatrī | [JB, 1, 272 4]
prāṇo vai priyam | [JB, 1, 272 5]
na vai prāṇāt preyaḥ kiṃ canāsti | [JB, 1, 272 6]
sa ya evam etāṃ gāyatrīṃ priyam upāste yathā priya eva prāṇa ātmana evaṃ priya eva sa kīrter evaṃ priyaś cakṣuṣa evaṃ priyaḥ saner bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 272 7]
atha hovāca jīvalaḥ kārīrādis triṣṭubham evāhaṃ śriyam upāsa iti | [JB, 1, 272 8]
kṣatraṃ vai triṣṭup | [JB, 1, 272 9]
kṣatraṃ vai śrīḥ | [JB, 1, 272 10]
sa ya evam etāṃ triṣṭubhaṃ śriyam upāste yasminn evārdhe bhavati tasya śreṣṭho bhavaty apy enaṃ rājāno 'dhastād upāsata iti | [JB, 1, 272 11]
atha hovācāṣāḍhaḥ sāvayaso jagatīm evāhaṃ bhūmānaṃ prajātim upāsa iti | [JB, 1, 272 12]
bhūmā vai prajātir jagatī chandasām | [JB, 1, 272 13]
sa ya evam etāṃ jagatīṃ bhūmānaṃ prajātim upāste bhūmānam eva prajayā paśubhir gacchati yatraiva sajāto bhavati tad grāmaṇīr bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 272 14]
atha hovācendradyumno bhāllabeyo 'nuṣṭubham evāhaṃ yaśa upāsa iti | [JB, 1, 272 15]
vāg vā anuṣṭup | [JB, 1, 272 16]
vāg u vai yaśaḥ | [JB, 1, 272 17]
vāg upary upary anyān kīrtiś carati | [JB, 1, 272 18]
sa ya evam etām anuṣṭubhaṃ yaśa upāsta eṣaivāsya vāg anuṣṭub upary upary evānyān kīrtir viharanty eti vivacanam eva bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 272 19]
{JB, 1, 273}
te ha vai te tathaikaikenaivāsuḥ | [JB, 1, 273 1]
atha ya evam etāni sarvāṇy ekadhā vedaivaṃ haitāni sarvāṇy ekadhā bhavanty ekadhaiva śreṣṭhaḥ svānāṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 273 2]
tad u hovāca vāsiṣṭhaś caikitāneyaḥ paścevānubudhya dhuro ha vā ime brāhmaṇā mīmāṃsamānās tām eva dhuraṃ nāvāgman yasyām etā dhuri sarvā adhīti | [JB, 1, 273 3]
retasyāṃ ha vai sa tad uvāca | [JB, 1, 273 4]
yāṃ ha vā āhur ekā dhūr iti retasyā ha vai sā dhurāṃ dhūḥ | [JB, 1, 273 5]
annaṃ tat | [JB, 1, 273 6]
dhurām alaṃkaraṇam | [JB, 1, 273 7]
surabhir gandho gāyatryai | [JB, 1, 273 8]
darśanīyas triṣṭubhaḥ | [JB, 1, 273 9]
śravaṇīyo jagatyai | [JB, 1, 273 10]
yadaiva vācā puṇyaṃ vadati tad anuṣṭubhaḥ | [JB, 1, 273 11]
sa ha vā enā annam ādadhāti ya enā etaiḥ samardhayati | [JB, 1, 273 12]
tā enam annādyamānā annādaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ svānāṃ kurvanti | [JB, 1, 273 13]
annādaś śreṣṭhaḥ svānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 273 14]
{JB, 1, 274}
trayo ha vā ete samudrā yat pavamānā agnir vāyur asāv ādityaḥ | [JB, 1, 274 1]
taiś channair udgāyet | [JB, 1, 274 2]
sa yarhi vai prajāpatiḥ prajābhyo vṛṣṭim annādyaṃ prayacchati chādyanta ete tarhi | [JB, 1, 274 3]
prajāpatir eṣa yad udgātā | [JB, 1, 274 4]
sa yat pavamānaiś channair udgāyati chādayaty eva yajamānam annādyena chādayaty ātmānaṃ chādayati prajāḥ | [JB, 1, 274 5]
bahuvarṣī tatra parjanyo bhavatīti ha smāha kūṭaś śailano yatrāham udgāyāmīti | [JB, 1, 274 6]
yatra vai bahuvarṣī parjanyo bhavati kalyāṇo vai tatra balīvardo 'śvataro hastī niṣkaḥ puruṣaḥ | [JB, 1, 274 7]
rūpaṃ rūpaṃ vāva tatra kalyāṇam ājāyata ity etaddha tad vidvān uvāca | [JB, 1, 274 8]
yo vai devāṃś ca manuṣyāṃś ca vyāvartayati vi pāpmanāvartate | [JB, 1, 274 9]
devā vai pavamānāḥ | [JB, 1, 274 10]
prajāḥ pṛṣṭhokthāni | [JB, 1, 274 11]
taiś channaiḥ parokṣam aniruktaiḥ pavamānair udgāyet | [JB, 1, 274 12]
channā iva hi parokṣam aniruktā iva devāḥ | [JB, 1, 274 13]
prajāḥ pṛṣṭhokthāni | [JB, 1, 274 14]
tair acchannaiḥ pratyakṣaṃ niruktair udgāyet | [JB, 1, 274 15]
acchannā iva hi pratyakṣaṃ niruktā iva manuṣyāḥ | [JB, 1, 274 16]
etad vai devāṃś ca manuṣyāṃś ca vyāvartayati vi pāpmanāvartate ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 274 17]
{JB, 1, 275}
daivīṃ ha vā eṣa saṃsadam eti yaḥ pavamānair udgāyati | [JB, 1, 275 1]
sa yathā śreyāṃsam abhyāyann evaṃ śikṣann ivopanamasyann iva saṃsiddhaiś śaknuvann upahanyamāna udgāyet | [JB, 1, 275 2]
yathāyantam āmīved yathā yad yācet tad dadyāt tādṛk tat | [JB, 1, 275 3]
atha ya etair asaṃsiddhair aśaknuvann anupahanyamāna udgāyed yathāyantaṃ pratimīved yathā yad yācet tan na dadyāt tādṛg u tat | [JB, 1, 275 4]
tad u hātraiva yajñasya samṛddhaṃ ca vyṛddhaṃ ca vijñāyate | [JB, 1, 275 5]
atihāryā ha vā eṣā yat pavamānāḥ | [JB, 1, 275 6]
yo vā atihāryām asaṃvīto 'tigāhate mṛdā vai sa lipyate nāyati vai | [JB, 1, 275 7]
atha yaḥ saṃvīto 'tigāhate na mṛdā lipyate na nāyati | [JB, 1, 275 8]
evam iva vai pavamānā upacaryāḥ | [JB, 1, 275 9]
tad āhur yad anyāni stotrāṇi stotriyapratipado 'tha kasmāt pavamānā astotriyapratipada iti | [JB, 1, 275 10]
sa brūyāt prāṇā vai pavamānāḥ | [JB, 1, 275 11]
prāṇā u pāvamānyaḥ | [JB, 1, 275 12]
tad yat pavamānān pāvamānībhir evānupratipadyeran parāñca eva prāṇān nirmṛjyur iti | [JB, 1, 275 13]
tān yad anuṣṭubhānupratipadyante vāg vā anuṣṭub vācy apāno niyato vācaiva tad apānaṃ dadhāra | [JB, 1, 275 14]
{JB, 1, 276}
tad āhur aśāntam iva vā etat stotraṃ yat stotriyeṇa nānupratipadyante | [JB, 1, 276 1]
kenaiṣāṃ stotriyapratipado 'nitaṃ bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 276 2]
sa brūyād vāg vā anuṣṭup | [JB, 1, 276 3]
vācy u vai sarvāṇi chandāṃsi | [JB, 1, 276 4]
yad āgneyam aindraṃ pavamānaṃ tenaiṣāṃ stotriyapratipado 'nitaṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 276 5]
jayā ha vai nāmaite stomā yat pavamānāḥ | [JB, 1, 276 6]
pavamānair vai devā asurān parāñca eva jayanta āyan | [JB, 1, 276 7]
tad yat pavamānāḥ parāñca eva bhavanti yathā parāṅ eva jayann iyāt tādṛk tat | [JB, 1, 276 8]
tān yad anuṣṭubhānupratipadyante vāg vā anuṣṭub vāg u vai vācayitrī vācā vā āha prehi jayābhikrāma māpakramīr iti | [JB, 1, 276 9]
sa yathā vācā brūyāt prehi jayābhikrāma māpakramīr iti tādṛk tat | [JB, 1, 276 10]
devā vai pavamānāḥ | [JB, 1, 276 11]
tāni devānāṃ stotrāṇi | [JB, 1, 276 12]
tāni devā anvāyattāḥ | [JB, 1, 276 13]
prajāḥ pṛṣṭhokthāni | [JB, 1, 276 14]
tāni prajānāṃ stotrāṇi | [JB, 1, 276 15]
tāni prajā anvāyattāḥ | [JB, 1, 276 16]
tad yat pavamānaiḥ parācīnair eva stuvate tasmāt parāñco devāḥ | [JB, 1, 276 17]
parāṅ āditya eti parāṅ candramāḥ parāñci nakṣatrāṇi parāṅ agnir dahann eti | [JB, 1, 276 18]
atha yasmāt pṛṣṭhokthaiḥ parācīnaiś cārvācīnaiś ca stuvate tasmād u parācīś cārvācīś ca prajāḥ | [JB, 1, 276 19]
parāñcaḥ prātaḥ prerate te sāyaṃ samāvartante | [JB, 1, 276 20]
parāg retaḥ siktaṃ tad arvāk prajāyate | [JB, 1, 276 21]
{JB, 1, 277}
pṛthur ha vainyo divyān vrātyān papraccha | [JB, 1, 277 1]
yajñasya dhāma paramaṃ guhāyāṃ nirmitaṃ mahato 'ntarikṣāt kasmād yanti pavamānāḥ parāñcaḥ kasmād ukthyāḥ punar abhyākanikradatīti | [JB, 1, 277 2]
devā anyāṃ vartanim adhvarasya mānuṣāsa upajīvanty anyāṃ tasmād yanti pavamānāḥ parāñcas tasmād ukthyāḥ punar abhyākanikradatīti ha pratyūcuḥ | [JB, 1, 277 3]
yo vai devān manuṣyeṣv ābhaktān veda manuṣyān u deveṣv ābhakta eva deveṣu bhavaty ābhakto manuṣyeṣu | [JB, 1, 277 4]
gacchati taṃ lokaṃ yatra devāḥ | [JB, 1, 277 5]
nāsmād devatā apakrāmanti | [JB, 1, 277 6]
devā vai pavamānāḥ | [JB, 1, 277 7]
prajāḥ pṛṣṭhokthāni | [JB, 1, 277 8]
sāma vai devāḥ | [JB, 1, 277 9]
prajāś chandāṃsi | [JB, 1, 277 10]
tad yat pavamānasāmāni parāñcy eva bhavanty atheyam ṛg anuniveṣṭate tena devā manuṣyeṣv ābhaktāḥ | [JB, 1, 277 11]
atha yad abhyāvartiṣv ṛcaṃ niveṣṭamānāṃ sāmānuniveṣṭate teno manuṣyā deveṣv ābhaktāḥ | [JB, 1, 277 12]
sa ya etad evaṃ vedābhakta eva deveṣu bhavaty ābhakto manuṣyeṣu | [JB, 1, 277 13]

nāsmād devatā apakrāmanti | [JB, 1, 277 15]
{JB, 1, 278}
yo vai devarūpaṃ ca manuṣyarūpaṃ ca vyāvartayati vi pāpmanāvartate | [JB, 1, 278 1]
devā vai pavamānāḥ | [JB, 1, 278 2]
prajāḥ pṛṣṭhokthāni | [JB, 1, 278 3]

tasyoddhāraḥ | [JB, 1, 278 12]
prajāpater evod uddhāraṃ harata uddhāryo bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 278 13]
tam etaṃ yajñasya rasaṃ pravṛhya purānyasmāt prajāpataye prayacchati tasmād bahiṣpavamānena stoṣyantaḥ prahvārā iva prakupitā iva sarpanti | [JB, 1, 278 14]
evam iva vai śreyasa upacāraḥ | [JB, 1, 278 15]
tasmād u tasya stotre na vyāharet | [JB, 1, 278 16]
ko hi śreyasaḥ pariveṣaṇam avavaditum arhati | [JB, 1, 278 17]
yo vai śreyasaḥ pariveṣaṇam avavadati yayā vai sa tam ārtyā kāmayate tayainaṃ ninayati | [JB, 1, 278 18]
atha yat tato 'dhvaryuḥ sampraiṣān vadati prajāpataya eva tad yajñasya rasaṃ pradāya tam āpyāyayati | [JB, 1, 278 19]
tenāsyāpīnena rasavatā stutaṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 278 20]
{JB, 1, 279}
yo vai devayaśasaṃ ca manuṣyayaśasaṃ ca veda yaśa eva deveṣu gacchati yaśo manuṣyeṣu | [JB, 1, 279 1]

devā vai pavamānāḥ | [JB, 1, 279 11]

prajāś śastrāṇi | [JB, 1, 279 14]
tad vā etat | [JB, 1, 279 15]

aṣṭau vasava ekādaśa rudrā dvādaśādityāḥ | [JB, 1, 279 18]
atha yasmād amitāni śastrāṇi tasmād v amitāḥ prajāḥ | [JB, 1, 279 19]
na tān vidma yāvanto brāhmaṇā yāvanto rājanyā yāvanto vaiśyā yāvantaś śūdrā iti | [JB, 1, 279 20]

mitaṃ ca hāsyāmitaṃ ca bahu bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 279 22]
ye arvāñcas taṃ u parāca āhur ye parāñcas taṃ u arvāca āhur indraś ca yā cakrathuḥ soma tāni dhurā na yuktā rajaso vahantīti | [JB, 1, 279 23]
pavamānā vai parāñcaḥ | [JB, 1, 279 24]

tasmāt prāṇyāpānituṃ śaknoti | [JB, 1, 279 27]
abhyāvartā arvāñcaḥ | [JB, 1, 279 28]
teṣāṃ parāñcaś camasāḥ | [JB, 1, 279 29]
te ha te 'pānā eva | [JB, 1, 279 30]

{JB, 1, 280}
yo vai savanānāṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ veda gacchati jyaiṣṭhyaṃ na jyaiṣṭhyād avarohati | [JB, 1, 280 1]
gāyatrī vai prātassavanasya jyaiṣṭhyam | [JB, 1, 280 2]

jagatī tṛtīyasavanasya jyaiṣṭhyam | [JB, 1, 280 6]

etad vai savanānāṃ jyaiṣṭhyam | [JB, 1, 280 8]

aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī | [JB, 1, 280 12]
aṣṭau vasavaḥ | [JB, 1, 280 13]

ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭup | [JB, 1, 280 15]
ekādaśa rudrāḥ | [JB, 1, 280 16]
triṣṭubhaiva rudrā gṛhiṇaḥ | [JB, 1, 280 17]
dvādaśākṣarā jagatī | [JB, 1, 280 18]
dvādaśādityāḥ | [JB, 1, 280 19]
jagatyaivādityā gṛhiṇaḥ | [JB, 1, 280 20]
anuṣṭubhaiva viśve devāḥ | [JB, 1, 280 21]
savanair indrāgnī | [JB, 1, 280 22]

{JB, 1, 281}
tad u ha smāheyapiḥ saumāpaḥ sa vādya yajeta sa vānyaṃ yājayed yo yathā mahati tīrthe 'sikate gā asaṃbādhamānāḥ saṃtarpayed evaṃ sarvā devatā anusavanaṃ chandassv akṣaram akṣaram anv asaṃbādhamānāḥ saṃtṛpyantīr vidyād iti | [JB, 1, 281 1]

{JB, 1, 282}
tad yatra ha vā evaṃvid yajata evaṃvid vā yājayati na haiva tasya devā īśate yat tan nāgaccheyuḥ | [JB, 1, 282 1]
yadi ca bhakṣayiṣyanto bhavanti yadi ca nātha haiva gacchanti | [JB, 1, 282 2]
yadi ha śucir bhavati bhakṣayanti | [JB, 1, 282 3]

taddhāpi paṇāyyaṃ yasya prekṣyaivāyan | [JB, 1, 282 5]

{JB, 1, 283}

{JB, 1, 284}
savanāny evendrāgnī anuprāviśatām | [JB, 1, 284 1]
tato vai tān mṛtyuḥ pāpmā na nirajānāt | [JB, 1, 284 2]
kuto hi tasya mṛtyuḥ pāpmeśiṣyate yaṃ na nirjānāti | [JB, 1, 284 3]
na hainaṃ mṛtyuḥ pāpmānuvindati ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 284 4]
chandāṃsi vāva tān mṛtyoḥ pāpmano 'cchādayan | [JB, 1, 284 5]
tad yad enāñ chandāṃsi mṛtyoḥ pāpmano 'cchādayaṃs tac chandasāṃ chandastvam | [JB, 1, 284 6]
chādayanty evainaṃ chandāṃsi mṛtyoḥ pāpmano ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 284 7]
tad yena yena ha vai chandasaivaṃvid ārtvijyaṃ karoti tat tad eva sa tarhi prapanno bhavati | [JB, 1, 284 8]
yena yena hy evainaṃ chandasā kurvantam upavadati tasmād āvṛścyate | [JB, 1, 284 9]
tasya haitasya naiva kā canārtir asti ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 284 10]
ya evainam upavadati sa ārtim ārcchati | [JB, 1, 284 11]
atha horjo jānāyanaḥ kapivanaṃ bhauvāyanaṃ papraccha yad gāyatraṃ prātassavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanam atha keyam anuṣṭub ayātayāmnī savanamukhāny upāpataty āntād yajñaṃ vahatīti | [JB, 1, 284 12]
sa hovāca vāg vā anuṣṭup | [JB, 1, 284 13]
vāco yajñas tāyate | [JB, 1, 284 14]
tad yathā vā ado bhadrabalīvardena rajjvabhihitena punaḥ punaḥ pratidhāvanti pratikūlāya vā gurave vodvoḍhava evaṃ vā etāṃ vācam anuṣṭubhaṃ savanamukheṣu pariyāṇāyaiva yuñjanti | [JB, 1, 284 15]
pratikūlānīva vā etāni yat savanamukhāni | [JB, 1, 284 16]
saiṣā vāg evāyātayāmny āntād yajñaṃ vahati | [JB, 1, 284 17]
yo vā anuṣṭubhaṃ sarvatrāpīdaṃ veda sarvatra hāsyāpi puṇye bhavati | [JB, 1, 284 18]
aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī | [JB, 1, 284 19]
ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭup | [JB, 1, 284 20]
dvādaśākṣarā jagatī | [JB, 1, 284 21]
vāg iti yajñāyajñīyasya nidhanam | [JB, 1, 284 22]
tad dvātriṃśat | [JB, 1, 284 23]
dvātriṃśadakṣarānuṣṭup | [JB, 1, 284 24]
api vā etasyai prātassavane 'pi mādhyaṃdine savane 'pi tṛtīyasavane | [JB, 1, 284 25]
api vā etasyai brahmaṇy api kṣatre 'pi viśi | [JB, 1, 284 26]
api vā etasyā asmin loke 'py antarikṣe 'py amuṣmin | [JB, 1, 284 27]
sa ya evam etām anuṣṭubhaṃ sarvatrāpīdaṃ veda sarvatra haivāsyāpi puṇye bhavati | [JB, 1, 284 28]
{JB, 1, 285}
atha hāhīnasam āśvatthiṃ keśī dārbhyaḥ keśinā sātyakāminā purodhāyā aparurodha | [JB, 1, 285 1]
sa ha sthavirataro 'hīnā āsa kumārataraḥ keśī | [JB, 1, 285 2]
taṃ hovācāṃ keśin kiṃ me vidvān rājanyam upāhṛthā iti | [JB, 1, 285 3]
sa hovācāṃ yad anuṣṭubham eva sarvāṇi chandāṃsy upāsmahe bṛhatīṃ paśūn yajñaṃ svargaṃ lokam iti | [JB, 1, 285 4]
taṃ hāṃsraṃ viveda | [JB, 1, 285 5]
sa ha kṛpayāṃcakre | [JB, 1, 285 6]
taṃ hovāca mā kṛpayathāḥ | [JB, 1, 285 7]
yadi rājanyakāmyā kṛpayasa eṣa te rājanyaḥ | [JB, 1, 285 8]
api vai vayam anyaṃ rājanyam eṣiṣyāmahā iti | [JB, 1, 285 9]
sa hovāca naitat keśin rājanyakāmyā | [JB, 1, 285 10]
brahmacaryam eva vai mā tad anusaṃsmṛtyāṃsram avidat | [JB, 1, 285 11]
cacāra vai brahmacaryam | [JB, 1, 285 12]
upajarasaṃ vāvedam aśṛṇma yad ayam iyatkumārako 'bhivedayata iti | [JB, 1, 285 13]
evam evaitad anusaṃsmṛtyāṃsram avidad iti | [JB, 1, 285 14]
sa yad anuṣṭubhaṃ sarvāṇi chandāṃsy uvāca | [JB, 1, 285 15]
aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī | [JB, 1, 285 16]
ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭup | [JB, 1, 285 17]
dvādaśākṣarā jagatī | [JB, 1, 285 18]
vāg iti yajñāyajñīyasya nidhanam | [JB, 1, 285 19]
tad dvātriṃśat | [JB, 1, 285 20]
dvātriṃśadakṣarānuṣṭup | [JB, 1, 285 21]
etad anuṣṭubhaṃ sarvāṇi chandāṃsy uvāca | [JB, 1, 285 22]
bṛhatīṃ paśūn iti | [JB, 1, 285 23]
yā vā anuṣṭup sā bṛhatī | [JB, 1, 285 24]
catuṣpātsu vā eṣā paśuṣūpahiteṣu bṛhaty abhavat | [JB, 1, 285 25]
yajñam iti | [JB, 1, 285 26]
yo hy eva paśumān bhavati taṃ yajña upanamati | [JB, 1, 285 27]
svargaṃ lokam iti | [JB, 1, 285 28]
bṛhatī hy eva svargo lokaḥ | [JB, 1, 285 29]
atha ha saṃgamanaḥ kṣaimiḥ satyayajñaṃ pauluṣiṃ papracchācāryeṇa prahita āruṇinā satyayajña pauluṣe yat stutā gāyatrī bhavati stūyate triṣṭub astutā jagatī kathaṃ tāḥ sarvāḥ sampadya mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanam udyacchantīti | [JB, 1, 285 30]

{JB, 1, 322}

{JB, 1, 323}

{JB, 1, 324}

{JB, 1, 325}
atha nirbādhāpastambhau | [JB, 1, 325 1]

tata eva sa parābhavati | [JB, 1, 325 3]
