tad u hovāca śāṭyāyanir apahatapāpmaitat sāmno yad ūrdhvaṃ prastāvāt | [JB, 1, 325 13]
svarga eṣa lokaḥ | [JB, 1, 325 14]
kas tasmin dviṣantaṃ bhrātṛvyam ābhajet | [JB, 1, 325 15]
prastuta eva purādeḥ sa evaiko nārakaḥ | [JB, 1, 325 16]
tad dviṣantaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ pātayitvā sarvasminn eva sāmann ātmānaṃ dadhyāt | [JB, 1, 325 17]
atho yajamānam | [JB, 1, 325 18]
so 'pahatya pāpmānaṃ svargaṃ lokam eti | [JB, 1, 325 19]
etat tad yat kṛtvā śreyān manyata iti | [JB, 1, 325 20]
{JB, 1, 326}
yo vā ṛksāmābhyām āyatanavadbhyām ārtvijyaṃ karoty āyatanavān bhavati | [JB, 1, 326 1]
prastāva evarcaḥ sāmann āyatanam | [JB, 1, 326 2]
yad ūrdhvaṃ prastāvāc channaṃ gāyati tat sāmna ṛcy āyatanam | [JB, 1, 326 3]
pratihāra evarcaḥ sāmann āyatanam | [JB, 1, 326 4]

nidhanam evarcaḥ sāmann āyatanam | [JB, 1, 326 6]
yan nidhanam atisvarati tat sāmna ṛcy āyatanam | [JB, 1, 326 7]
sa ya evam etābhyām ṛksāmābhyām āyatanavadbhyām ārtvijyaṃ karoty āyatanavān eva bhavati | [JB, 1, 326 8]
tad vā etad dvayam evark caiva sāma ca | [JB, 1, 326 9]
tayor yat satyaṃ prajāsu bhavati jayati taṃ lokaṃ yaḥ satyena jeyaḥ | [JB, 1, 326 10]
vāg vā ṛcaḥ satyam | [JB, 1, 326 11]
manaḥ sāmnaḥ | [JB, 1, 326 12]
ete ha vā ṛksāmayoḥ satye | [JB, 1, 326 13]
satyaṃ prajāsu bhavati jayati taṃ lokaṃ yaḥ satyena jeyaḥ | [JB, 1, 326 14]
ṛcaḥ satyena sāma gāyāt | [JB, 1, 326 15]
sāmnaḥ satyenarcam | [JB, 1, 326 16]
ṛksāmne u ha vai svargasya lokasyeśāte | [JB, 1, 326 17]
taṃ ha vā ete svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayataḥ | [JB, 1, 326 18]
sa svargasya lokasyeśe ya ene evaṃ gāyati | [JB, 1, 326 19]
tasmād evam eva geye | [JB, 1, 326 20]
{JB, 1, 327}
rathantareṇa stoṣyamāṇaḥ pṛthivīm abhimṛśati namo mātre pṛthivyai rathantara mā mā hiṃsīr iti | [JB, 1, 327 1]
atha mahimnaḥ saṃbharati yas te agnau mahimā yas te apsu rathe yas te mahimā stanayitnau ya u te vāte yas te mahimā tena saṃbhava rathantara draviṇasvan na edhīti | [JB, 1, 327 2]
atha vāmadevyaṃ purastāc chāntim abhivyāharati prajāpatir asi vāmadevya brahmaṇaś śaraṇa tan mā pāhīti | [JB, 1, 327 3]
athaitā amṛtavyāhṛtīr abhivyāharati bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ ka idam udgāsyati sa idam udgāsyatīti | [JB, 1, 327 4]
prajāpatir vai kaḥ | [JB, 1, 327 5]
tam evādāv ārtvijyāya vṛṇīte | [JB, 1, 327 6]
sa ya eva tad udgāyati vācaivāsya kṛtaṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 327 7]
anṛṇa ātmanā bhavati | [JB, 1, 327 8]
athābhyaniti | [JB, 1, 327 9]
prāṇo vai śāntiḥ | [JB, 1, 327 10]
agnir vai bṛhadrathantare | [JB, 1, 327 11]
te prāṇena śamayati | [JB, 1, 327 12]
atha ye 'śānte bṛhadrathantare gāyanti te haite yuvānaś śrotriyāḥ pramīyante svayam upariṣṭād vāmadevyam | [JB, 1, 327 13]
{JB, 1, 328}
sa yathā gharmaṃ taptaṃ śaphābhyāṃ parigṛhya hared evam evaitad bṛhadrathantare vāmadevyābhyāṃ parigṛhya harati | [JB, 1, 328 1]
te enaṃ nodoṣataḥ | [JB, 1, 328 2]
sa sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃ vidvān bṛhadrathantare gāyati | [JB, 1, 328 3]
iyaṃ vai rathantaram | [JB, 1, 328 4]
tasyā asau vatso yo 'sau tapati | [JB, 1, 328 5]

sa yathā dhenuṃ vatsenopasṛjya prattāṃ duhītaivam evaitena gītena rathantaraṃ duhe yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate | [JB, 1, 328 7]
śrīr vai rathantaram | [JB, 1, 328 8]
tasyā ime stobhā yad asyāṃ pṛthivyām adhi | [JB, 1, 328 9]
saiṣā śrīr nānyatrākṣarebhya āptavyā | [JB, 1, 328 10]

sā haiṣaikasthā śrīr yad akṣareṣu | [JB, 1, 328 12]
tasmād akṣareṣu stobdhavyam | [JB, 1, 328 13]
{JB, 1, 329}
tad etad amūlaṃ rathantaraṃ yad anyatrākṣarebhyaḥ | [JB, 1, 329 1]

tasmād akṣareṣv eva stobdhavyam | [JB, 1, 329 4]
devatāgāyinaḥ kurupañcālā āyatanād acyavanteti ha smāha śāṭyāyaniḥ | [JB, 1, 329 5]
mano vai pūrvam atha vāk | [JB, 1, 329 6]
mano vai bṛhad vāg rathantaram | [JB, 1, 329 7]
tad yatra bṛhadrathantare ājim aitāṃ tad bṛhad udajayat | [JB, 1, 329 8]
rathantaraṃ hīyamānam amanyata | [JB, 1, 329 9]

sa ha kṣipre pāpmānaṃ vijahāti ya evaṃ vidvān kṣipraṃ rathantaraṃ gāyati | [JB, 1, 329 12]
{JB, 1, 330}

{JB, 1, 331}
ṣoḍaśākṣarāṇi stobhati | [JB, 1, 331 1]

caturdaśa caturdaśottarayoḥ | [JB, 1, 331 5]

sa ha sa vajra ūnonārambhaṇaḥ | [JB, 1, 331 17]

{JB, 1, 332}

agnir eṣa yad rathantaram | [JB, 1, 332 3]

svardṛśam iti nirāha | [JB, 1, 332 10]

{JB, 1, 333}
athaitad vāmadevyam | [JB, 1, 333 1]
ā pratihārād anavānaṃ geyam | [JB, 1, 333 2]
prāṇo hi vāmadevyam | [JB, 1, 333 3]

no hānyasyānuvartma geyam | [JB, 1, 333 5]

sāmāni hy asmāt sṛṣṭāni | [JB, 1, 333 9]
yathā jaratkośo vā syād aśvataro vā vicchidvahāḥ | [JB, 1, 333 10]
pṛṣṭhaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ hi prativahatīti | [JB, 1, 333 11]
tasmin pṛṣṭharūpaṃ vā gāyed etā vā vyāhṛtīr vyāhṛtyodgāyed gauś cāśvaś cājā cāviś ca vrīhiś ca yavaś ceti | [JB, 1, 333 12]
gaur eva rathantaram | [JB, 1, 333 13]
aśvo bṛhat | [JB, 1, 333 14]
ajā vairūpam | [JB, 1, 333 15]

vrīhayaś śakvaryaḥ | [JB, 1, 333 17]
yavā revatayaḥ | [JB, 1, 333 18]
tad ye 'smād rasāt sṛṣṭā bhavanti tān asmin dadhāti | [JB, 1, 333 19]
tad āpyāyayati | [JB, 1, 333 20]
tenāsyāpīnena rasavatā stutaṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 333 21]
sa yadi vṛṣṭikāmaḥ syād āpo vāyur āpo vāyur iti purastād vyāhṛtya vāmadevyena stuvīta | [JB, 1, 333 22]
tatho haivāsmai varṣati | [JB, 1, 333 23]
atho paśavo vai vāmadevyam | [JB, 1, 333 24]
sa paśumān bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān vāmadevyena stute | [JB, 1, 333 25]
taddha vai sugītaṃ brahmasāmno yad enad brahmalokaiḥ sampādyodgāyati | [JB, 1, 333 26]
sapta kṛtvo brahmasāmnaḥ prarohati | [JB, 1, 333 27]
saptama u loke brahma | [JB, 1, 333 28]
vāsor māndāno vā iti catuḥ prārukṣat | [JB, 1, 333 29]
āndhāsā bhī vātsān no vā iti triḥ | [JB, 1, 333 30]
tat sapta sampadyante | [JB, 1, 333 31]
{JB, 1, 334}
upodako nāma loko yasminn ayam agniḥ | [JB, 1, 334 1]
ṛtadhāmā yasmin vāyuḥ | [JB, 1, 334 2]
aparājito yasminn ādityaḥ | [JB, 1, 334 3]
adhidyur yasmin varuṇaḥ | [JB, 1, 334 4]
pradyur yasmin mṛtyuḥ | [JB, 1, 334 5]
rocano yasminn aśanāyā | [JB, 1, 334 6]
viṣṭapa eva saptamo brahmaloko yasminn etad brahma | [JB, 1, 334 7]

atho yajamānam | [JB, 1, 334 9]

{JB, 1, 335}
athaitat kāleyam | [JB, 1, 335 1]
vistṛṇann iva vyavasāyayann ivāsaṃrundhann iva gāyet | [JB, 1, 335 2]
yathā yavācitaṃ vā svācitaṃ yāyān māṣācitaṃ veti ha sma purā kurūṇāṃ brāhmaṇā mīmāṃsanta evam etad yat kāleyam | [JB, 1, 335 3]
tad vikarṣateva geyam iti | [JB, 1, 335 4]

vāyur vāmadevyam | [JB, 1, 335 11]
indro naudhasam | [JB, 1, 335 12]
viśve devāḥ kāleyam | [JB, 1, 335 13]
athaiṣa svarga eva loko viśva eva devāḥ | [JB, 1, 335 14]
svarga eva tal loke viśveṣu deveṣu pratitiṣṭhanti | [JB, 1, 335 15]

tasmād eṣā nitataiveḍāntata upetyā sarvāyuṣṭāyā asya lokasyānudghātāyeti | [JB, 1, 335 17]
{JB, 1, 336}
athaitat saṃhitaṃ brahma savanamukhe kriyate | [JB, 1, 336 1]
tad etat svayampraśastaṃ yad brahma | [JB, 1, 336 2]
tasminn u praśasta eva saty eṣā bhūyasī praśaṃsā kriyate yad etad om ity ādatte | [JB, 1, 336 3]
asāv āditya etad akṣaram | [JB, 1, 336 4]
tad etat trayasya vedasyāpīḍitam akṣaram | [JB, 1, 336 5]
sa yad om ity ādatte 'mum evaitad ādityaṃ mukha ādhatte | [JB, 1, 336 6]

tad āpyāyayati | [JB, 1, 336 8]
tenāsyāpīnena rasavatā stutaṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 336 9]
pratihriyamāṇaṃ sāmāvasīdatīty āhuḥ kuravaḥ | [JB, 1, 336 10]
sa yad ūrdhvaṃ pratihārād udgṛhṇāti tad utthāpayatīti | [JB, 1, 336 11]
sāmann u haivaitat sāmābhigīyate | [JB, 1, 336 12]
taddha vai sugītam | [JB, 1, 336 13]

{JB, 1, 337}
athaite uṣṇikkakubhāv ā pratihārād anavānaṃ geye | [JB, 1, 337 1]
saṃśīrṇam ivaitac chandaḥ | [JB, 1, 337 2]
puruṣacchandasaṃ hy uṣṇikkakubhau | [JB, 1, 337 3]
taddha śamastomī bālākiḥ sāyakaṃ jānaśruteyam antevāsinam udgāpayan svayajñe 'nuvyājahāra | [JB, 1, 337 4]
tathā nvā ayaṃ jānaśruteyaḥ sāmāgāsīd yathāsyedānīṃ rudhiram utpatiṣyatīti | [JB, 1, 337 5]
atha hājinavāsino yudhyamānāḥ sadaḥ prapeduḥ | [JB, 1, 337 6]
tasya ha daṇḍaḥ patitvā rudhiram utpātayāṃcakāra | [JB, 1, 337 7]
sa hovācātha kathaṃ gāyed iti | [JB, 1, 337 8]
tasmai haitad uvācāsṛg ity eva na nirdyotayet | [JB, 1, 337 9]
ho ity eva gāyet | [JB, 1, 337 10]
no ha sarvaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ channaṃ gāyet | [JB, 1, 337 11]
yo hainaṃ chādayantaṃ brūyād adhakṣan vā ayam udgātātmānaṃ ca yajamānaṃ ceti tathā haiva syāt | [JB, 1, 337 12]
dṛṃhyām eva nirdyotayet | [JB, 1, 337 13]
dṛṃhīmān iti vai praśaṃsanti | [JB, 1, 337 14]
athaitac chyāvāśvam | [JB, 1, 337 15]
aiho vā ehi yā ity evaite gāyanti | [JB, 1, 337 16]
vāg eṣā | [JB, 1, 337 17]
vāg anuṣṭup | [JB, 1, 337 18]
vācy etad vācā pratitiṣṭhāmeti | [JB, 1, 337 19]
taddha tathā gāyantaṃ brahmadattaṃ caikitāneyaṃ gaḍūnā ārkṣākāyaṇo 'nuvyājahāra | [JB, 1, 337 20]

{JB, 1, 358}
sa vai khalu prajāpatir yajñaṃ sṛṣṭvordhva udakrāmat | [JB, 1, 358 1]

saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [JB, 1, 358 11]

saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [JB, 1, 358 13]
atha yadīṣṭipaśubandheṣu vā darśapūrṇamāsayor vā bhuvaḥ svāhety anvāhāryapacane juhavātha | [JB, 1, 358 14]
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [JB, 1, 358 15]

anayā trayyā vidyayeti ha brūyāt | [JB, 1, 358 22]

{JB, 1, 359}
tad āhur yat pūrvapakṣaṃ manuṣyāḥ sunvanty aparapakṣaṃ devā atha sattriṇa ubhau pūrvapakṣāparapakṣau sunvanta āsate yo nvāvaikena manuṣyeṇa saṃsunoti taṃ nv eva paricakṣate | [JB, 1, 359 1]
atha kiṃ ya ubhayair devamanuṣyaiḥ | [JB, 1, 359 2]
kathaṃ teṣāṃ tad asaṃsutaṃ bhavatīti | [JB, 1, 359 3]
sa brūyād amuṃ vai lokaṃ manuṣyāḥ pūrvapakṣe vardhayanty amum āpyāyayanty amuṃ prajanayanti | [JB, 1, 359 4]
pūrvapakṣe yajamāno vidyād amum idaṃ lokaṃ vardhayāmy amum āpyāyayāmy amuṃ prajanayāmi | [JB, 1, 359 5]
devānām anuṣeṇo 'smīti | [JB, 1, 359 6]
yo vai śreyaso 'nuṣeṇo bhavati na vai sa riṣyati | [JB, 1, 359 7]
imam u vai lokaṃ devā aparapakṣe vardhayantīmam āpyāyayantīmaṃ prajanayanti | [JB, 1, 359 8]
aparapakṣe yajamāno vidyād imam idaṃ lokaṃ vardhayāmīmam āpyāyayāmīmaṃ prajanayāmi | [JB, 1, 359 9]
manuṣyāṇām anuṣeṇo 'smīti | [JB, 1, 359 10]
yo vai śreyaso 'nuṣeṇo bhavati na vai sa riṣyati | [JB, 1, 359 11]
{JB, 1, 360}
atha ha smāha bhāllabeya imaṃ ha vai lokaṃ devā aparapakṣe vardhayantīmam āpyāyayantīmaṃ prajanayanti | [JB, 1, 360 1]
tasmāt pra pūrvāḥ prajāḥ paśava oṣadhayo vanaspatayo daghyante 'thāparāḥ kalyāṇītarāḥ kalyāṇītarāḥ pratidhīyanta iti | [JB, 1, 360 2]
etaddha tad vidvān uvāca | [JB, 1, 360 3]
tad āhur yad rathāhnyaṃ vā nadīṃ vā giribhidam asaṃsavaṃ manyante 'tha sattriṇaḥ sāmānyāṃ śālāyāṃ bahavaḥ sunvanta āsate yadi vai te manyante nānedaṃ yajāmahā iti saṃ tarhi sunvanti | [JB, 1, 360 4]
yady u vai manyante gṛhapatim idaṃ yājayāma ity antaritās tarhi yajñād bhavanti | [JB, 1, 360 5]
kathaṃ teṣāṃ tan nāneṣṭaṃ bhavati katham asaṃsutam iti | [JB, 1, 360 6]
sa brūyāt | [JB, 1, 360 7]
{JB, 1, 361}
prāṇo vai somo rājā | [JB, 1, 361 1]
tad yaddhavirdhāne grāvabhiḥ somaṃ rājānam abhiṣutya nānāgrahān gṛhṇanti nānāpravarān pravṛṇate nānā yajanti tenaivaiṣāṃ tan nāneṣṭaṃ bhavati | [JB, 1, 361 2]
atho yad evaiṣā samānā satī devatā nānā prajāsu pratiṣṭhitā teno asaṃsutam iti | [JB, 1, 361 3]
yo ha tvai saṃsave saṃsavaṃ veda sa haiva saṃsunvator abhibhavati | [JB, 1, 361 4]
ayam eva yo 'yaṃ pavata eṣa eva saṃsave saṃsave | [JB, 1, 361 5]
etaṃ hi sarve devā anuyanti | [JB, 1, 361 6]
tasmād yām eṣa diśaṃ vāti tāṃ diśam oṣadhayo vanaspatayo 'nupratighnate | [JB, 1, 361 7]
sa eṣa vā āpaḥ | [JB, 1, 361 8]
yadā hy evarcchaty atha varṣaṃs tiṣṭhati | [JB, 1, 361 9]
sa eva tāv antareṇāvakāśaḥ | [JB, 1, 361 10]
saiva sā nadī giribhid bhavaty asaṃsavāya | [JB, 1, 361 11]
tasmād u haivaṃ vidvān apy utkāśe dīkṣeta | [JB, 1, 361 12]
sa haiva saṃsunvator abhibhavati | [JB, 1, 361 13]
sa etāṃ devatām upatiṣṭheta śivo 'si pra tvā padye namas te 'stu mā mā hiṃsīr yo māṃ dveṣṭi sa ārtim ārcchatv iti | [JB, 1, 361 14]
yo haivaivaṃvidaṃ dveṣṭi sa ārtim ārcchati | [JB, 1, 361 15]
{JB, 1, 362}
tad āhuḥ katidhāvakīryamāṇaḥ praviśatīti | [JB, 1, 362 1]
caturdheti brūyāt | [JB, 1, 362 2]
caturdhā ha vā eṣa praviśati yo 'vakīryata indraṃ balena marutaḥ prāṇena bṛhaspatiṃ brahmavarcasenāgnim evetareṇa sarveṇa | [JB, 1, 362 3]
athāśukraḥ pariśiṣyate | [JB, 1, 362 4]
tasyaiṣā prāyaścittiḥ | [JB, 1, 362 5]
amāvāsyāṃ rātrim agnim upasamādhāya paristīrya pariṣicyaite āhutī juhuyāt | [JB, 1, 362 6]
kāmāvakīrṇo 'smy avakīrṇo 'smi kāma kāmāya svāhā | [JB, 1, 362 7]
kāmābhidrugdho 'smy abhidrugdho 'smi kāma kāmāya svāheti | [JB, 1, 362 8]
so 'ñjaliṃ kṛtvā trir upatiṣṭhatu | [JB, 1, 362 9]
saṃ mā siñcantu marutaḥ sam indraḥ saṃ bṛhaspatis saṃ māyam agniḥ siñcatv āyuṣā ca balena ca dīrgham āyuḥ kṛṇotu ma iti | [JB, 1, 362 10]
sa yad āha saṃ mā siñcantu maruta iti maruta evāsmai tat punaḥ prāṇaṃ dadati ya evaṃ veda tasmai | [JB, 1, 362 11]
sa yad āha sam indra itīndra evāsmai tat punar balaṃ dadāti ya evaṃ veda tasmai | [JB, 1, 362 12]
sa yad āha saṃ bṛhaspatir iti bṛhaspatir evāsmai tad brahmavarcasaṃ dadāti ya evaṃ veda tasmai | [JB, 1, 362 13]
sa yad āha sam agnir ity agnir evainaṃ tat sarveṇetareṇa samardhayati yenāvakīryamāṇo vyṛdhyate | [JB, 1, 362 14]
sa trir abhimantrayate | [JB, 1, 362 15]
traya ime lokāḥ | [JB, 1, 362 16]
āpnotīmāṃs trīn lokān sarvam āyur ety ava pāpmānaṃ hate gacchati svargaṃ lokam | [JB, 1, 362 17]
{JB, 1, 363}
atha ha vai naimiśīyā iti sattriṇo 'yasthūṇagṛhapatayaḥ sattraṃ niṣeduḥ | [JB, 1, 363 1]
teṣāṃ mahendro vyardhayiṣyan markaṭarūpeṇa puroḍāśaṃ pramamātha | [JB, 1, 363 2]
atha haiṣāṃ śitibāhur aiṣakṛto 'dhvaryur anūcāna āsa | [JB, 1, 363 3]
sa haitaṃ trayyai vidyāyai śukraṃ rasaṃ pravṛḍhaṃ vidāṃcakāra sarvasya prāyaścittiṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar ity etābhir vyāhṛtibhiḥ | [JB, 1, 363 4]
etā vai vyāhṛtayaḥ sarvaprāyaścittayaḥ | [JB, 1, 363 5]
tad yathā vā adaḥ samudro 'nanto 'pāro 'kṣito dyāvāpṛthivī sarva ime lokā evaṃ vā etā vyāhṛtayo 'kṣitāḥ | [JB, 1, 363 6]
{JB, 1, 364}
adugdhā anantā apārā iti | [JB, 1, 364 1]
tad yad vai bhūr iti tad ayaṃ lokaḥ | [JB, 1, 364 2]
yad bhuva iti tad idam antarikṣam | [JB, 1, 364 3]
yat svar iti tad asau lokaḥ | [JB, 1, 364 4]
etā vai vyāhṛtaya etā devatāḥ | [JB, 1, 364 5]
etā devatā etā vyāhṛtaya ity etaddha tadviduṣaś śitibāhor aiṣakṛtasya naimiśer markaṭaḥ puroḍāśaṃ pramamātha | [JB, 1, 364 6]
sa hovāca caturgṛhītam ājyaṃ gṛhītvā vā hara juhomi veti | [JB, 1, 364 7]
sa hovāca tad u ha tvam itthaṃ cāmuthā cāsa yadi tvam anūciṣe markaṭaḥ puroḍāśaṃ pramathiṣyati tasya prāyaścittim iti | [JB, 1, 364 8]
sa hovāca tad ahāhaṃ vasīyān bhūyāsaṃ yad aham anvabruvy asamājñātasya prāyaścittim ā vā hara juhomi veti | [JB, 1, 364 9]
āharāṇīti hovāca mā hauṣīr iti | [JB, 1, 364 10]
tam u hājahāra | [JB, 1, 364 11]
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān brahmā bhavati dakṣiṇato hāsyodaṅ yajñaḥ pravaṇo bhavati | [JB, 1, 364 12]
dakṣiṇato hāsyodaṅ yajñaḥ pravaṇaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate yasyaivaṃ vidvān brahmā bhavati ya u cainam evaṃ veda ya u cainam evaṃ veda | [JB, 1, 364 13]
{JB, 2, 1}
vāg eṣā yat pṛṣṭhāni | [JB, 2, 1 1]
tām etāṃ viprayuñjate | [JB, 2, 1 2]
tāṃ viharanti | [JB, 2, 1 3]
sā prathamam ahaḥ prāpya rathantaraṃ bhavati | [JB, 2, 1 4]
iyam eva pṛthivī | [JB, 2, 1 5]
vāg vai rathantaram | [JB, 2, 1 6]
saiṣāvadati | [JB, 2, 1 7]
sā dvitīyam ahaḥ prāpya bṛhatī bhavati yām imāṃ śreṣṭhī vācaṃ vadatīty avocad iti | [JB, 2, 1 8]
sā hi dūrācchrūyate | [JB, 2, 1 9]

sā caturtham ahaḥ prāpya virāḍ bhavati | [JB, 2, 1 11]
tūṣṇīṃ niṣadyam | [JB, 2, 1 12]
etaddha vai vairājyaṃ vāco yat tūṣṇīṃ niṣadyaṃ yām imāṃ śreṣṭhinas tūṣṇīm āsīnasyaiva jijñāsante | [JB, 2, 1 13]
sā pañcamam ahaḥ prāpya śakvarī bhavati yayā praśiṣṭaḥ śaknoti | [JB, 2, 1 14]
sā ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ prāpya revatī bhavati yayānnādyaṃ pradīyate | [JB, 2, 1 15]
sā na māsi māsy āttavyā | [JB, 2, 1 16]
lelibhasyaitad ājānaṃ yām imāṃ lelibhā vācaṃ vadanti | [JB, 2, 1 17]
imāṃ vā ayaṃ hyo 'vadad imāṃ pūrvedyur imāṃ pūrvasamām | [JB, 2, 1 18]
samānīṃ bata vācaṃ vadati na batainaṃ paryetīti | [JB, 2, 1 19]
evaṃ tad yan māsi māsi pṛṣṭhāny upayanti | [JB, 2, 1 20]
{JB, 2, 23}

tasmād dīkṣitān sata āhur āsata iti yady api te śayīrann athottiṣṭheyuḥ | [JB, 2, 23 3]
agnir hi devānām āsīnānāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ | [JB, 2, 23 4]
agnidevatyā hi tarhi bhavanti | [JB, 2, 23 5]
tasmād utthitān sata āhur udasthur iti yady api ta āsīrann atho śayīran | [JB, 2, 23 6]
ādityo hi devānām utthitānāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ | [JB, 2, 23 7]
ādityadevatyā hi tarhi bhavanti | [JB, 2, 23 8]

ta etad ṛgretasaṃ yajūretasaṃ brahmaṇi yonau reto dadhato yanti | [JB, 2, 23 11]

taruṇam iva tarhi reto bhavati | [JB, 2, 23 14]

taruṇam iva hi tarhi reto bhavati | [JB, 2, 23 16]
tān stutiśastrais trir vardhayanto 'bhiśṛṇvanto yanti | [JB, 2, 23 17]
tasmād garbhā anaśnataḥ sambhavanti | [JB, 2, 23 18]
{JB, 2, 41}
atha ha vai trayaḥ pūrve 'gnaya āsur bhūpatir bhuvanapatir bhūtānāṃ patiḥ | [JB, 2, 41 1]
ayaṃ vai loko bhūpatir antarikṣaṃ bhuvanapatir asāv eva loko bhūtānāṃ patiḥ | [JB, 2, 41 2]
atha hāyaṃ bhūtir nāma | [JB, 2, 41 3]
teṣāṃ ha vaṣaṭkāraḥ śīrṣāṇi cicheda | [JB, 2, 41 4]
ta imās tisraḥ pṛthivīḥ praviviśuḥ | [JB, 2, 41 5]
tasmād yad agnihotrasya vājyasya vāvaskandet tad abhimṛśed bhūpataye svāhā bhuvanapataye svāhā bhūtānāṃ pataye svāheti | [JB, 2, 41 6]
eteṣu haivāsyāgniṣu hutam askannaṃ bhavati | [JB, 2, 41 7]
atha ha vai trayaḥ pūrva ṛṣaya āsuḥ śūrpaṃyavam adhvānā antarvān kṛṣiḥ solvālāḥ | [JB, 2, 41 8]
te ha yajñasya kṛntatrāṇi dadṛśuḥ | [JB, 2, 41 9]
tasyaitāḥ prāyaścittīr dadṛśuḥ śaṃ ca ma upa ca ma āyuś ca me bhūyaś ca me yajña śivo me saṃtiṣṭhasva yajña sviṣṭo me saṃtiṣṭhasva yajñāriṣṭo me saṃtiṣṭhasveti | [JB, 2, 41 10]
tasmād etā darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ vā cāturmāsyair vā paśubandhena vā saumyena vādhvareṇeṣṭvopariṣṭāj japet | [JB, 2, 41 11]
yad evātra yajñasya vidhuraṃ bhavati tad eva tena śamayati | [JB, 2, 41 12]
prāṇa evāviṣuvato vyāno viṣuvān apāno yad ūrdhvaṃ viṣuvataḥ | [JB, 2, 41 13]
apāno vā idaṃ sarvam āharati | [JB, 2, 41 14]
tasmād vayaṃ parastād viṣuvato 'rvācaḥ ṣaḍahān upaimaḥ | [JB, 2, 41 15]
{JB, 2, 64}

annaṃ vai vicakṣaṇam | [JB, 2, 64 2]

annam u somaḥ | [JB, 2, 64 6]

tasya vāg eva mithunam | [JB, 2, 64 10]
mithunavatīm eva tad vācaṃ vadati | [JB, 2, 64 11]
vicakṣaṇavatīṃ vācaṃ vadati | [JB, 2, 64 12]
annaṃ vai vicakṣaṇam | [JB, 2, 64 13]
annena hīmāḥ prajā vipaśyanti | [JB, 2, 64 14]
tata ābhyaḥ prajābhyo 'nnādyaṃ prayacchati | [JB, 2, 64 15]
sa yadāsmai vrataṃ prayacchet sarvam eva vratayet sarvasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyai | [JB, 2, 64 16]
yady u pariśiṃṣyād vratapradaṃ brūyād aśāna vā piba veti | [JB, 2, 64 17]
yadya u vrataprado 'nucchiṣṭāśī vā syāt pari vā śiṃṣyāt tad adbhir abhyukṣya chāyāyāṃ niṣektavai brūyāt | [JB, 2, 64 18]
tad oṣadhībhir abhisaṃchādayitavai brūyāt | [JB, 2, 64 19]
tad oṣadhīnāṃ mūlāny upasiñcati | [JB, 2, 64 20]

dīkṣitā udaśūśuṣann itīhāhuḥ | [JB, 2, 64 22]

sā dīkṣamāṇasyendriyaṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ śraiṣṭhyaṃ yaśa ādatse | [JB, 2, 64 24]

{JB, 2, 129}
sa trivṛd rathantarasāmā bhavati | [JB, 2, 129 1]
brahma vai trivṛd brahma rathantaram | [JB, 2, 129 2]
brahmaṇā vāva sa tad brahmavarcasam ārdhnot | [JB, 2, 129 3]
brahmaṇaiva brahmavarcasam ṛdhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 2, 129 4]
tasya trayastriṃśad dakṣiṇā bhavanti | [JB, 2, 129 5]
trayastriṃśad vai devatāḥ | [JB, 2, 129 6]
devatānām eva purodhām āśnuta | [JB, 2, 129 7]
aśvaś catustriṃśaḥ | [JB, 2, 129 8]
prajāpater vā etad rūpaṃ yad aśvaḥ | [JB, 2, 129 9]
saprajāpatikānām eva tena devatānāṃ purodhām āśnuta | [JB, 2, 129 10]
tasyaitā yathāpūrvam anusavanaṃ dakṣiṇā dadāty aṣṭau prātassavane dadāty ekādaśa mādhyaṃdine savane dvādaśa tṛtīyasavane 'nūbaṃdhyāyām ekām | [JB, 2, 129 11]
udavasānīyāyām ekām | [JB, 2, 129 12]
anusavanam aśvaṃ tṛtīyaśaḥ | [JB, 2, 129 13]

atha yām anūbaṃdhyāyām ekāṃ mitrāvaruṇayor eva tena purodhām āśnuta | [JB, 2, 129 17]
atha yām udavasānīyāyām ekāṃ karma karma me dakṣiṇāvad asad iti | [JB, 2, 129 18]
atha yam anusavanam aśvaṃ tṛtīyaśaḥ prajāpater eva tena purodhām āśnuta | [JB, 2, 129 19]
{JB, 2, 153}
triśīrṣā ha vai tvāṣṭra āsa | [JB, 2, 153 1]

sa u hāsurīputra āsa | [JB, 2, 153 6]

{JB, 2, 154}

{JB, 2, 155}
taṃ ha vajrahasto 'bhidudrāva | [JB, 2, 155 1]

taṃ ha tatra nānuprapede | [JB, 2, 155 3]

udeyāyendraḥ | [JB, 2, 155 6]

sa hekṣāṃcakre dṛḍhaṃ bata ma ṛṣayo yācanti | [JB, 3, 203 16]
na hājajñāv akūpāraṃ didṛkṣanta iti | [JB, 3, 203 17]
yan manyase vareṇyam indra dyukṣaṃ tad ā bhara | [JB, 3, 203 18.1]
vidyāma tasya te vayam akūpārasya dāvane | [JB, 3, 203 18.2]
iti | [JB, 3, 203 18.3]
sa hājajñāv akūpāraṃ vai didṛkṣanta iti | [JB, 3, 203 19]
taṃ ha padodasyann uvācedam eva medam ṛṣayo mahad ivobhayāhasty ā bharety avocann iti | [JB, 3, 203 20]
tam apaśyan | [JB, 3, 203 21]
tā etāḥ kāmasanaya ṛcaḥ | [JB, 3, 203 22]
etaṃ vai te kāmam akāmayanta | [JB, 3, 203 23]
sa ebhyaḥ kāmaḥ samārdhyata | [JB, 3, 203 24]
yatkāma evaitābhir ṛgbhi stute sam asmai sa kāma ṛdhyate | [JB, 3, 203 25]
{JB, 3, 273}
athākūpāram | [JB, 3, 273 1]
akūpāro vai kaśyapaḥ kalibhiḥ saha samudram abhyavaiṣat | [JB, 3, 273 2]
tasmin pratiṣṭhām aicchat | [JB, 3, 273 3]
sa etat sāmāpaśyat | [JB, 3, 273 4]
tenāstuta | [JB, 3, 273 5]
tato vai sa samudre pratiṣṭhām avindatemām eva pṛthivīm | [JB, 3, 273 6]
tato ha sma vai tasya kalayaḥ pṛṣṭha āsate | [JB, 3, 273 7]
tad etat pratiṣṭhāsāma | [JB, 3, 273 8]
pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 3, 273 9]
samudro vai chandomāḥ | [JB, 3, 273 10]
kaśyapo vai samudram atipārayitum arhati | [JB, 3, 273 11]
tad yad atrākūpāraṃ bhavati samudrasyaivātipāraṇāya | [JB, 3, 273 12]
yad v akūpāraḥ kaśyapo 'paśyat tasmād ākūpāram ity ākhyāyate | [JB, 3, 273 13]
athaitā dvipado bhavanty uktabrāhmaṇāḥ | [JB, 3, 273 14]
tā etā bhavanti pavasva soma mahe dakṣāyeti | [JB, 3, 273 15]
mahaddhy etad ahar yad aṣṭācatvāriṃśam | [JB, 3, 273 16]
tāsu vidharmoktabrāhmaṇam | [JB, 3, 273 17]
tac caturakṣaraṇidhanaṃ bhavati catuṣpadā vai paśavaḥ | [JB, 3, 273 18]
paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām evāvaruddhyai | [JB, 3, 273 19]
upo ṣu jātam apturam iti janadvatīr bhavanti | [JB, 3, 273 20]
janadvad vai jagatyai rūpam | [JB, 3, 273 21]
jāgatam etad ahaḥ | [JB, 3, 273 22]
gobhir bhaṃgaṃ pariṣkṛtam | [JB, 3, 273 23]
induṃ devā ayāsiṣuḥ | [JB, 3, 273 24]
arṣā nas soma śaṃ gave dhukṣasva pipyuṣīm iṣam | [JB, 3, 273 25]
vardhā samudram ukthyam | [JB, 3, 273 26]
iti gomatīḥ paśumatīr bhavanti paśūnām evāvaruddhyai | [JB, 3, 273 27]
paśavo hi chandomāḥ | [JB, 3, 273 28]
tam id vardhantu no gira iti vṛddhaṃ hy etad ahar yad aṣṭācatvāriṃśam | [JB, 3, 273 29]
{JB, 3, 346}
tad yathā vṛkṣaṃ vā giriṃ vādhiruhya vyavekṣetaivam evaitasmāllokād anyān lokān vyavekṣate | [JB, 3, 346 1]
sa imāḥ prajā aśanāyantīḥ pratyavaikṣata | [JB, 3, 346 2]
tā dvābhyāṃ rūpābhyāṃ pratyādravan nīlena ca suvarṇena ca | [JB, 3, 346 3]
tad yat parjanyasya varṣiṣyataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ tannīlam | [JB, 3, 346 4]
atha yad apsv antar vidyotate tat suvarṇam | [JB, 3, 346 5]
tābhyo 'varṣat | [JB, 3, 346 6]
tata odano 'jāyata | [JB, 3, 346 7]
tam aśitvodānan | [JB, 3, 346 8]
sa udano 'bhavat | [JB, 3, 346 9]
tad udanasyodanatvam | [JB, 3, 346 10]
udano ha vai nāmaiṣa | [JB, 3, 346 11]
tam odana iti parokṣam ācakṣate | [JB, 3, 346 12]
dvitīyaṃ jyāyo 'nnādyam ajāyata | [JB, 3, 346 13]
tad abhisaṃpadya vyamathnata | [JB, 3, 346 14]
sa mantho 'bhavat | [JB, 3, 346 15]
tan manthasya manthatvam | [JB, 3, 346 16]
tad etad dvayam evānnādyasya rūpaṃ yaccaivāśnāti yacca pibati | [JB, 3, 346 17]
yad aśnāty odanasya tad rūpaṃ yat pibati manthasya tat | [JB, 3, 346 18]
ubhayaṃ hāsyaitad gṛhe 'dhigamyate ya evaṃ veda | [JB, 3, 346 19]
tau haitau prajāpater eva stanau yad vrīhiś ca yavaś ca | [JB, 3, 346 20]
tābhyām imāḥ prajā bibharti | [JB, 3, 346 21]
